本文件代替 GB 18030 一 2005 信息技术 ”中文编码字符集与 GB 18030 一 2005 相比,除结构调整和编辑性改动外,主要扩术变化如下:	This document replaces GB 18030 - 2005 Information Technology "Compared with GB 18030 - 2005, except for restructuring and editorial changes, the main changes in expansion are as follows.	yes

在四字节编码区更改了18 个 GB/T 13000 代码位置(见附录 D,2005 年版的附录D);	18 GB/T 13000 code positions have been changed in the four-byte coding area (see Appendix D, Appendix D of the 2005 edition).	yes

1 本文件规定了信息技术用的中文图形字符及甚二进制编码的十六进制表示 。	1 This document specifies the hexadecimal representation of the Chinese graphic characters and the very binary code for information technology use.	yes
本文件适用于中文和其他文字图形字符信息的处理、交换、存储、传给、显现 、输入和输出。	This document applies to the Chinese and other text graphics character information processing, exchange, storage, transmission, display, input and output.	no
本文件适用于为具备中文和其他文字图形字符信息化处理及交换功能的技术类产品,包括但不限于以输入法、光学字符识别 (OCR)、编辑 校对、机融翻诺、语音合成、文字转写、乔能写作等为代表的软件产品 , 以及以计算机、通信终端设备、电子书阅读毅、学习机等为代表的便件产品 。	This document applies to technical products with the function of information processing and exchange of Chinese and other text and graphic characters, including but not limited to software products represented by input method, optical character recognition (OCR), editing and proofreading, machine fusion and flipping, speech synthesis, text transcription, and Qiaoneng writing, etc., and convenience products represented by computers, communication terminals, e-books, e-books, and learning machines.	no

4 字汇	4 Word Exchange	no
4.1 概述	4.1 General	no
本文件收录的字符以单字节、双字或四字节编码 。	Characters included in this document are encoded as single, double or quadruple bytes .	no
单字节部分收录了 GB/T 11383 一 1989 的 0x00~0x7F 全部 128 个字符 。	The single-byte part includes all 128 characters from 0x00 to 0x7F of GB/T 11383-1989.	no
4.3 双字节部分	4.3 Double-byte sections	no
双字节部分收录了 GB/T 2312 一 1980 中的全部图形字符 GB/T 13000 中的CJK 统一汉字以及部分图形字符。	The double-byte part includes all the graphic characters in GB/T 2312 and 1980, the CJK unified Chinese characters in GB/T 13000, and some graphic characters.	no
双字节部分的字符按照附录 A 的规定。	Characters in the double-byte section are as specified in Appendix A.	no
其中,表意文字描述符的图形、代码位置和功能应符合附录 B 的规定 。	Among them, the graphics, code positions and functions of ideographic descriptors shall be in accordance with the provisions of Appendix B.	no
注: GB/T 13000 对中国、日本、恩国、越南等国家和地区使用的汉字统一编码。	Note: GB/T 13000 is a unified code for Chinese characters used in China, Japan, Japan, Vietnam and other countries and regions.	no
具备独有抽象字形的汉字,赋予单独的代码位置;来源不同而抽象字形相同的汉字, 则赋予共用的代码位置。	Chinese characters with unique abstract glyphs are assigned separate code positions; Chinese characters with the same abstract glyphs from different sources are assigned common code positions.	no
经过编码的汉字称为CJK 统一汉字 CCJK Unified Ideographs,其中 CJK 表示中国、日本、韩国。	The encoded Chinese characters are called CJK Unified Chinese Characters CCJK Unified Ideographs, where CJK stands for China, Japan, and Korea.	no
4.4 四字节部分	4.4 Quadruple Byte Sections	no
四字节部分收录了上述双字节字符之外的 GB/T 13000 中的 66 个CJK统一汉字(9FA6 一 9FEF，不包括 9FB4~9FBB 的8个字符)、CJK 统一汉字扩充 A、CJK 统一汉字扩充 BCJK 统一汉字扩充 C、 CJK 统一汉字扩充 DCJK 统一汉字扩充下 .CJK 统一汉字扩充 F 和已经 在 GB/ 工 13000 中编码的少数民族文字的字符。	The four-byte part includes the 66 CJK unified Chinese characters in GB/T 13000 other than the double-byte characters mentioned above (9FA6-9FEF, excluding the 8 characters from 9FB4-9FBB), CJK unified Chinese character expansion A, CJK unified Chinese character expansion BCJK unified Chinese character expansion C, CJK unified Chinese character expansion DCJK unified Chinese character expansion under .CJK unified Chinese character expansion F and the characters of minority characters already encoded in GB/IT 13000. CJK Unified Kanji Expansion under .CJK Unified Kanji Expansion F and the characters of ethnic minority scripts already encoded in GB/IW 13000.	no
四字节部分的字符按照附录 C 的规定 。	Characters in the four-byte section are as specified in Appendix C.	no
5 总体结构	5 Overall structure	no
正文中凡数字前标有 0x 的表示采用十六进制,未标有 0x 的表示采用十进制。	In the text, any number preceded by 0x is in hexadecimal, and any number not preceded by 0x is in decimal.	no
附录中凡编码的表示均采用十六进制,其他数字的表示均采用十进制。	All codes in the appendix are expressed in hexadecimal, and all other numbers are expressed in decimal.	no
单字节部分采用 GB/T 11383 一 1989 的编码结构,使 用 0x00~0x7F 码位。	The single-byte part adopts the coding structure of GB/T 11383-1989, using 0x00~0x7F code bits.	no
双字贡部分采用两个八位二进制位串表示一个字符,其首字节码位从 0x81 一 0xFE, 尾字节码位分别是 0x40 一 0x7E 和 0x80 一 0xFE。	The double-word tribute part uses two eight-bit binary bit strings to represent a character, the first byte code bits from 0x81 to 0xFE, and the last byte code bits are 0x40 to 0x7E and 0x80 to 0xFE, respectively.	no
四字节部分采用 GB/工 11383 一 1989 未采用的 0x30 一 0x39 作为对双字节编码扩充的后缀,编码范围为 0x81308130 一 0xFE39FE39。	The four-byte part adopts 0x30 and 0x39, which is not adopted in GB/I 11383-1989, as the suffix of double-byte encoding expansion, and the encoding range is 0x81308130 and 0xFE39FE39.	no
四字节字符的第一个字厄编码范围为 0x81 一 0xFE;第二个字记编码范围为 0x30 一 0x39; 第三个字节编码范围为 0x81 一 0xFE;第 四个字市编码范围为 0x30 一 0x39。 即 : 0x81308130 一 0x81308139; 0x81308230 一 0x81308239 0x8130FEFE30 一 0x8130FE39 ; 0x81318130 一 0x81318139 ; Oo2douolag0c “0URo23061393 0xFE39FE30 一 0xFE39FE39 。	The first byte of a four-byte character is encoded as 0x81 1 0xFE; the second is encoded as 0x30 1 0x39; the third is encoded as 0x81 1 0xFE; and the fourth is encoded as 0x30 1 0x39. i.e. 0x81308130 0x81308130; 0x81308230 0x81308239; 0x81308230; 0x81308239; 0x8130FE39; 0x81318130; 0x81318139; Oo2douolag0c "0 0x81308239; 0x81318130 0x81318139 0x81308239 0x8130FEFE30 a 0x8130FE39 ; 0x81318130 a 0x81318139 ; Oo2douolag0c "0URo23061393 0xFE39FE30 a 0xFE39FE39 .	no
总体结构与码位范围分配见图 1 和表 1。	The overall structure and code range assignments are shown in Figure 1 and Table 1.	no
6 字符的排列顺序	6 Order of characters	no
6.1 单字刷部分字符的排列顺序	6.1 Arrangement order of some characters in the monogram brush	no
单字记部分字符按照 GB/I 11383 一 1989 中相应字符的顺序排列 。	The characters of the single character notation are arranged in the order of the corresponding characters in GB/I 11383-1989.	no
6.2 双字市部分字符的排列顺序	6.2 Ordering of some characters in double-letter cities	no
双字下部分字符排列顺序应符合附录 A。	The order of the characters in the lower part of the double word shall be in accordance with Appendix A.	no
6.3 四字刷部分字符的排列顺序	6.3 Order of characters in the four-character brush section	no
自 0x81308130 至 0x8439FE39 共 50400 个码位,对应双字节部分未包括的所有 GB/T 13000 基本多文种平面的字符,按照GB/T13000 基本多文种平面相应字符的顺序排列 。	From 0x81308130 to 0x8439FE39, there are 50400 code bits, corresponding to all the characters of GB/T 13000 basic multilingual plane not included in the double-byte part, and they are arranged in the order of the corresponding characters of GB/T13000 basic multilingual plane.	no
自 0x90308130 至 0xE339FE39 共 1058400 个码位用于对应 GB/T 13000 的16个辅助平面,字符排列顺序完全按照 GB/I 13000 的 16个辅助平面的相应码位顺序依次排列 。	From 0x90308130 to 0xE339FE39, a total of 1058400 code bits are used to correspond to the 16 auxiliary planes of GB/T 13000, and the characters are arranged in the order of the corresponding code bits of the 16 auxiliary planes of GB/I 13000.	no
四字节部分字符排列顺序应符合附录 C。	The order of characters in the four-byte section shall be in accordance with Appendix C.	no

描述 (DESCRIPTION) C 和 C++ 编译器是集成的.他们都要用四个步骤中的一个或多个处理输入文件: 预处理(preprocessing), Hii(compilation), (assembly) MERE (linking) .	DESCRIPTION The C and C++ compilers are integrated. They both process input files in one or more of four steps: preprocessing, compilation, assembly, and linking.	yes
源文件后级名标识源文件的语言, 但是对编译器来说, 后绥名控制着缺省设定:	The source filename identifies the language of the source file, but for the compiler, the sui generis name controls the default setting.	yes
gcc 认为预处理后的文件(.i) 是 c 文件, 并且设定 c 形式的连接，	gcc considers the preprocessed file (.i) to be a c-file, and sets up a c-form link.	yes

在连接阶段中,所有对应于源程序的.e 文件，-1 库文件, 无法识别的文件名(包括指定的.o H 标文件和 .a 库文件)按命令行中的顺序传递给连接器选项 (OPTIONS)	During the linking phase, all .e files corresponding to the source program, -1 library files, and unrecognizable filenames (including specified .o H files and .a library files) are passed to the connector options in the order they appear on the command line.	no
选项必须分立给出 : de ' 完全不同于 `-d -r '.	The options must be given separately : de ' is completely different from `-d -r '.	no
大多数 ` -=E :和 `-W' 选项有两个相反的格式 : -fname 和 -fno-name (或 -Wname 和 -Wno- name).	Most ` -=E :and `-W' options have two opposite formats : -fname and -fno-name (or -Wname and -Wno- name).	no

这个选项应用于后面所有的输入文件, 直到遇着下一个 `-x' 选项 .language 的可选	This option is applied to all subsequent input files, until the next `-x' option, .language, is encountered.	yes

如果只操作四个阶段( 预处理, 编译, 汇编, 连接)中的一部分, 可以使用 ` -x' 选项 (或文件名后 Ah) 告诉 geo 从哪里开始,用 `~-c' ，`-s' ,或 `-E' 选项告诉 geo 到哪里结束.注意,某些选项组合 (例如 ，`-x cpp-output -E') {i gee MEF =c 编译或汇编源文件, ETER. If only part of the four stages (preprocessing, compiling, assembling, linking) is to be manipulated, the ` -x' option (or Ah after the filename) can be used to tell geo where to start, and the `~-c', `-s', or `-E' options can be used to tell geo where to end. Note that some combinations of options (e.g., `-x cpp-output -E') {i gee MEF =c compiles or assembles the source file, ETER. ERA ATI By default, GCC labels the file with ` .ec' after the source filename by replacing it with ` .o'. GCC ignores any unrecognized input text after the -ec option -S F anything.	yes
了的目标文件.	The objective of the document is to provide a clearer picture of the situation in the country.	yes
编译后即停止, 不进行汇编件.	Stop after compilation, no assembly.	yes
在编译过程的不同阶段间使用管道而非临时文件进行工作, 因为那些系统的汇编器不能从管道读取数据，GNU 的汇编器没有这个问题，汇编器能够接受的 C "方言 ": 支持符合 ANSI 标准的 C 程序.	Work with pipes instead of temporary files between different stages of the compilation process, because the assembler of those systems can not read data from pipes, GNU's assembler does not have this problem, the assembler is able to accept the C "dialect": support for ANSI-compliant C programs.	yes
这样就会关闭 GNU Cc 中某些不兼容 ANSI Cc 的特性关键字, 以及诸如 unix 和 vax 这些表明当迎和极少使用的 ANSI trigraph 特性,以及禁上尽管使 用了(译注 :宿主环境 (hosted environment) 下所有的标准库可用，main 函数返回 一个 int 值, 典型例子是除了内核以外几乎所有的程序.对应的独立环境 (f£reestanding environment) 不存在标准库, 程序入口也不一定是 main, 最明显的例子就是操作系统内核.详情参考 gcc 网站最近的资料)	This turns off certain keywords in GNU Cc that are not ANSI Cc-compatible features, as well as ANSI trigraph features such as unix and vax, which are welcome and rarely used, and the main function, which returns an int value, even though it is disabled for use in all the standard libraries available in the hosted environment. Typical examples are almost all programs except the kernel. The corresponding f£reestanding environment has no standard libraries, and the entry point to a program is not necessarily main, the most obvious example being the operating system kernel. (For more information, see the recent information on the gcc website).	yes
对于没有参数的函数声明, 例如 `int foo ();', 按 C 风格处理 --- 即不说明参数个数或类型. (仅针对 C++) .	Function declarations without arguments, e.g. `int foo ();', are handled in the C style - i.e. without specifying the number or type of arguments. (C++ only) .	no
正常情况下, 这样的函数 foo 在 C++ 中意味着参数为空.	Normally, such a function foo means that the argument is empty in C++.	no
节清单从这里删到试图支持传统 C 编译器的某些方面.	The list of sections from which to delete attempts to support some aspects of the traditional C compiler.	no
详见NU c 手册,我们已经把细节删除, 这样当内容过时后, 人们也不会 HERI.	See the NU c manual for details, which we've removed so that people won't HERI when the content becomes obsolete.	no
除了一件事: 对于 c++ 程序 (不是C)，` -traditional' 选项带来一个附加效应,允许对 this 赋值.	Except for one thing: for c++ programs (not C), the ` -traditional' option has the added effect of allowing this to be assigned a value.	no
他和`-Ethis-is-variable' 选项的果一样.	He has the same effect as the `-Ethis-is-variable' option.	no
-traditional-cpp 试图支持传统 Cc 预处理器的某些方面.	-traditional-cpp attempts to support some aspects of the traditional Cc preprocessor.	no
特别是上面提到有关预处理器的内容, 但是不包括 `-traditional' 选项的其他效应.	In particular, the preprocessor is mentioned above, but not the other effects of the `-traditional' option.	no
-fdollars-in-identifiers 允许在标识符 (identifier) 中使用 `$' 字符 (仅针对 C++) .	-fdollars-in-identifiers allows `$' characters in identifiers (C++ only) .	no
你可以指定 `“-Efno-dollars-in-identifiers' 选项显明禁止使用 `$' 符.	You can specify the `"-Efno-dollars-in-identifiers' option to explicitly disable the `$' character.	no
(GNU C++ 在某些目标系统缺省允许 `$' 符, 但不是所有系统.)	(GNU C++ allows the `$' character by default on some target systems, but not all.)	no
-fenum-int-equiv 允许 ant 类型到枚举类型 (enumeration) 的隐式转换 (MEF c++) .	-fenum-int-equiv Allows implicit conversion of ant types to enumeration types (MEF c++) .	no
正常情况下 GNU C++ 允许从 enum 到 int 的转换,反之则不行.	Normally GNU C++ allows conversions from enum to int, but not vice versa.	no
-fexternal-—templates 为模板声明 (template declaration) 产生较小的代码 (仅限于 c++)，方法是对于每个模板函数 (template function),只在 定义他们的地方生成一个副本.	-fexternal--templates Produces smaller code for template declarations (c++ only) by generating a copy of each template function only in the place where they are defined.	no
想要成功使用这个选项, 你必须在所有使用模板的文件中,标记`#pragma implementatio'(定义)或 `#Pragma interface'(声明).	To use this option successfully, you must mark `#pragma implementatio' (definition) or `#Pragma interface' (declaration) in all files that use the template.	no
程序用 `-fexternal-templates ' 编译时, 模板实例 (template instantiation) 全部是外部类型.你必须让需要的实例在实现文件中出现.	When the program is compiled with `-fexternal-templates ', the template instantiation is all external. You must make the required instances appear in the implementation file.	no
可以通过 typedef 实现这一点, 他引用所需的每个实例.	This can be accomplished with a typedef, which references each instance needed.	no
相对应的, 如果编译时使用缺省选项 ` -fno-exteznal-templates', 所有模板实例明确的设为内置.	In contrast, if compiled with the default option ` -fno-exteznal-templates', all template instances are explicitly built-in.	no
所有的成员函数(除了构造子函数和 mnew 或 delete 成员操作符) 视为所在类的虚函数.	All member functions (except constructors and the mnew or delete member operators) are considered virtual functions of their class.	no
这不表明每次调用成员函数都将通过内部虚函数表.	This does not mean that every call to a member function will go through the internal virtual function table.	no
有些情况下, 编译器能够判断出可以直接调用某个虚函数; 这时就直接调用.	In some cases, the compiler is able to determine that a virtual function can be called directly; then it is called directly.	no
-fcond-mismatch 允许条件表达式的第二和第三个参数的类型不匹配.	-fcond-mismatch Allows type mismatches between the second and third arguments of a conditional expression.	no
这种表达式的值是 Void.-fthis-—is-variable 允许对 this 赋值 (仅对 c++).	The value of such an expression is Void.-fthis--is-variable allows assignment of a value to this (only for c++).	no
合并用户自定义的自由存储管理机制到 c++ 后,使可赋值的`this' 显得不合时宜.	Merging a user-defined free storage management mechanism into c++ makes the assignable `this' obsolete.	no
因此, 默认情况下, 类成员函数内部对 this 赋值是无效操作.	Thus, by default, assigning a value to this inside a class member function is an invalid operation.	no
然而为了向后兼容, 你可以通过 `-fthis-is-variable' 选项使这种操作有效.	However, for backward compatibility, you can make this work with the `-fthis-is-variable' option.	no
-funsigned-char 把 char 定义为无符号类型,如同 unsigned char.	-funsigned-char Defines a char as an unsigned type, like an unsigned char.	no
各种机器都有自己缺省的 char 类型. 既可能是 unsigned char 也可能是 signed char.	Each machine has its own default char type. It can be either an unsigned char or a signed char.	no
理想情况下, 当依赖于数据的符号性时, 一个可移植程序总是应该使用 signed char 或 unsigned chaz.	Ideally, a portable program should always use signed char or unsigned chaz when relying on the signed nature of the data.	no
但是许多程序已经写成只用简单的 char, 并且期街这是有符号数(或者无符号数, 具体情况取决于编写程序的目标机器).	But many programs have been written to use just a simple char, and expect it to be signed (or unsigned, depending on the target machine for which the program is written).	no
这个选项, 和它的反义选项, 使那样的程序工作在对应的默认值上.	This option, and its inverse, makes the program work with the corresponding default values.	no
char 的类型始终应该明确定义为 signed char 或 unsigned char, 即使它表现的和其中之一完全一样.	The type of a char should always be explicitly defined as either signed char or unsigned char, even if it behaves exactly like one of them.	no
如果没有明确声明 ` signed' 或 "unsigned'修饰符, 这些选项用来定义有符号位域 (bitfield) 或无符号位域.	If the ` signed' or `unsigned' modifiers are not explicitly declared, these options are used to define either a signed bitfield or an unsigned bitfield.	no
缺省情况下,位域是有符号的, 因为他们继承的基本整数类型,如 int,是有符号数，然而, 如果指定了 `-traditional' 选项,位域永远是无符号数.	By default, bitfields are signed because the basic integer types they inherit from, such as int, are signed; however, if the `-traditional' option is specified, bitfields are always unsigned.	no
-fwritable-strings把字符串常量存储到可写数据段, 而且不做特别对待.	-fwritable-strings stores string constants in a writable segment, and does not treat them as such.	no
这是为了兼容一些老程序,他们算改字符串常量是一个非常糟糕的想法、`-traditional' 选项也有相同效果.	This is for compatibility with some older programs, where changing string constants is a very bad idea, and the `-traditional' option has the same effect.	no
执行摘要	Executive summary	yes
新冠肺炎对毒品市场的影响	Impact of New Crown Pneumonia on Drug Markets	yes
其影响可能类似于2008年的经济危机	The impact could be similar to the economic crisis of 2008	yes
全球性的新冠肺炎疫情已使全世界陷入前所未有的危机。	The global epidemic of new coronavirus pneumonia has plunged the world into an unprecedented crisis.	yes
在许多国家，这一疾病己使医疗服务机构穷于应付，几近崩溃，各国政府实施的限制措施已在全球经济中造成了严重紊乱。	In many countries, the disease has overwhelmed and nearly collapsed health-care services, and the restrictions imposed by Governments have caused serious disruptions in the global economy.	yes
对于毒品市场，这场疫情的影响尚不清楚，也很难预测，但有可能影响深远。	For the drug market, the impact of this epidemic is unclear and difficult to predict, but it has the potential to be far-reaching.	yes
一些生产者可能会被迫寻找新的方法来制造毒品，因为限制流动的同时也限制了前体和基本化学品的获取。	Some producers may be forced to find new ways to manufacture drugs because restrictions on movement also limit access to precursors and essential chemicals.	yes
贩运者由于旅行限制而无法越境，可能不得不寻找新的路线和方法。	Traffickers who are unable to cross borders due to travel restrictions may have to find new routes and methods.	yes
毒品使用和提供的模式可能会改变，政府的应对能力也可能会受到阻碍。	Patterns of drug use and availability may change and the ability of Governments to respond may be hampered.	yes
新冠肺炎带来的转变是前所未有的，但还是可以从以往的危机中吸取一些经验教训。	The transformation brought about by the new Crown Pneumonia is unprecedented, but there are still some lessons to be learned from previous crises.	yes
2008年经济危机后，一些吸毒者开始寻找更便宜的合成物质，使用模式转向注射毒品。	After the economic crisis of 2008, some drug users began to look for cheaper synthetic substances and the pattern of use shifted to injecting drugs.	no
与此同时，各国政府削减了与毒品相关的预算。	At the same time, Governments have cut drug-related budgets.	no
如果各国政府以同样的方式应对当前的经济衰退，预防吸毒和相关风险行为等干预措施和戒毒治疗服务可能会受到沉重打击。	Interventions such as prevention of drug use and related risk behaviours and drug treatment services may be hit hard if Governments respond to the current economic downturn in the same way.	no
此外，拦截行动和国际合作的优先性可能会降低，使贩运者更容易行动。	In addition, interception operations and international cooperation may be prioritized less, making it easier for traffickers to act.	no
一些国家有大量毒品通过商业航班走私，预计这些国家的贩毒活动受到的直接影响最大。	A number of countries where large quantities of drugs are smuggled on commercial flights are expected to be the most directly affected by drug trafficking.	no
有信使将甲基苯丙胺等合成毒品放在随身背包或藏在私人行李中携带，有时数量很大。由于几乎各地都对航空客运实施了限制，利用商业航空旅行供应毒品的活动可能会完全中断。	Synthetic drugs such as methamphetamine are carried by couriers in carry-on backpacks or concealed in personal luggage, sometimes in large quantities. The use of commercial air travel for the supply of drugs may be completely disrupted by the restrictions imposed on passenger air transportation almost everywhere.	no
尽管国际邮政供应链也受到了干扰，但利用暗网和货物邮寄进行贩运的活动可能会增加。	Although the international postal supply chain has also been disrupted, there may be an increase in the use of the dark web and the mailing of goods for trafficking purposes.	no
从长远来看，经济衰退和相关的封闭措施可能会打乱毒品市场。	In the long run, the recession and related closures may disrupt the drug market.	no
由于不断上升的失业率和缺乏机会，贫困和弱势人群将更有可能以有害的方式吸毒，患上吸毒病症，并转向与毒品有关的非法活动一无论是生产还是运输。	As a result of rising unemployment and lack of opportunities, poor and vulnerable people will be more likely to use drugs in a harmful way, develop drug use disorders and turn to illicit drug-related activities, whether production or transportation.	no
贩毒组织可能会利用这种情况，向脆弱人群提供服务，并招募新成员来壮大队伍。	Drug-trafficking organizations may take advantage of this situation by providing services to vulnerable populations and recruiting new members to swell their ranks.	no
随着政府应对能力的降低，这些转变可能会快速扎根，成为许多社区的新现实。	These shifts are likely to take root quickly and become a new reality for many communities as government response capacity diminishes.	no
扩张与复杂性	Expansion and Complexity	no
市场增长	market growth	no
人口增长模式部分解释了市场扩张的原因	Population growth patterns partially explain market expansion	no
世界各地的吸毒现象一直在增多，无论是从总体数字还是从吸毒者在世界人口中所占比例来看都是如此。	Drug abuse has been on the rise around the world, both in terms of overall figures and as a percentage of the world's population.	no
2009年估计吸毒者有2.1亿人，占全球15-64岁人口的4.8%,而2018年估计吸毒者有2.69亿人，占这类人口的5.3%。	In 2009, there were an estimated 210 million drug users, accounting for 4.8 per cent of the global population aged 15-64, while in 2018, there were an estimated 269 million drug users, accounting for 5.3 per cent of that population.	no
在过去二十年期间，发展中国家吸毒情况的增长速度远远快于发达国家。	During the past two decades, drug abuse in developing countries has grown much faster than in developed countries.	no
这在一定程度上反映了这一期间总体人口增长的差异、发达国家为7%,发展中国家为28%但也反映了发展中国家年 轻人口增长较快。	This reflects, to some extent, the differences in overall population growth over the period, which varied from 7 per cent in developed countries to 28 per cent in developing countries, but also reflects the faster growth of the young population in developing countries.	no
青少年和年轻成年人在吸毒者中所占比例最大。	Adolescents and young adults make up the largest proportion of drug users.	no
在2000-2018年期间，发展中国家这一年龄段的人口增长了16%,而发达国家这一年龄段的人口减少了10%。	During the period 2000-2018, the population in this age group in developing countries increased by 16 per cent, while the population in this age group in developed countries decreased by 10 per cent.	no
1城市化是当前和未来毒品市场的一个驱动因素	1 Urbanization as a driver of current and future drug markets	no
无论是发达国家还是发展中国家，城市地区的吸毒情况都多于农村地区。	In both developed and developing countries, drug use is more prevalent in urban areas than in rural areas.	no
吸毒情况总体增多的部分原因是人口从农村向城镇的大规模流动一目前全世界人口有一半以上生活在城市地区，而1960年这一比例为34%。	The overall increase in drug use is partly due to the large-scale movement of people from rural to urban areas, with more than half of the world's population now living in urban areas, compared with 34 per cent in 1960.	no
城市化可能是毒品市场未来动态的一个关键因素，特别是在城市化趋势更为突出的发展中国家。	Urbanization is likely to be a key factor in the future dynamics of drug markets, especially in developing countries where the trend towards urbanization is more pronounced.	no
财富的增加与吸毒情况增多相联，但承受疾病负担最大的是最贫穷的人在世界范围内，发达国家的吸毒情况比发展中国家更为普遍。	Increased wealth is associated with increased drug use, but it is the poorest people who bear the greatest burden of disease and, worldwide, drug use is more prevalent in developed countries than in developing countries.	no
可卡因之类的毒品更是与世界上较富裕的地区联系较为牢固。	Drugs such as cocaine are even more strongly associated with wealthier parts of the world.	no
同样，在各国内部，社会富裕阶层的吸毒流行率较高。	Similarly, within countries, the prevalence of drug use is higher among the wealthier segments of society.	no
但转为吸毒病症的比率较高的却是社会经济地位较低的人。	However, the rate of transition to drug use disorders is higher among people of lower socio-economic status.	no
来自少数几个国家的数据表明，有害的吸毒模式与病症同低收入之间存在联系。	Data from a small number of countries suggest that there is a link between harmful patterns of drug use and morbidity and low incomes.	no
这些模式在较富裕的社会阶层似乎不太常见。	These patterns appear to be less common in more affluent segments of society.	no
全球新冠肺炎危机造成的经济制约很可能会加剧包括吸毒者在内的最弱势群体的风险。	The economic constraints caused by the global NCRP crisis are likely to exacerbate the risks for the most vulnerable groups, including drug users.	no
例如，劳动力市场的变化，如失业率上升，过去一直与吸毒情况的增加有关，而这场疫情己经迫使全球数千万人失业。	For example, changes in the labor market, such as rising unemployment, have been linked in the past to increased drug use, and the epidemic has forced tens of millions of people out of work globally.	no
新冠肺炎或将导致毒品市场进一步扩张新冠肺炎的大流行可能会导致更多农民增加或从事非法作物种植，或是因为国家主管机关的控制能力降低，或是因为在经济危机之下可能有更多人不得不铤而走险，从事非法活动。	CKP may lead to further expansion of the drug market The CKP pandemic may lead to more farmers increasing or engaging in illicit crop cultivation, either because of a reduced capacity of State authorities to control it or because more people may be forced to take risks and engage in illicit activities in the context of the economic crisis.	no
新冠肺炎的相关限制措施导致空中和陆路交通减少，海上贩运可能已经因此而增加，海上的拦截风险低，而且比空中或陆路走私的数量更多。	Restrictions related to NCRP have led to a decrease in air and land traffic, and trafficking by sea may have increased as a result, with the risk of interception at sea being low and greater than that of smuggling by air or land.	no
最近已有报告称可卡因货物直接从南美经由海路运往欧洲。	There have been recent reports of cocaine consignments being transported directly from South America to Europe by sea.	no
复杂性增强	Increased complexity	yes
非国际管制物质的出现情况稳定，但有潜在危害的新型类阿片正在增多毒品市场正日趋复杂。	The emergence of substances not under international control has stabilized, but new and potentially harmful opioids are on the rise and the drug market is becoming increasingly complex.	yes
除大麻、可卡因和海洛因等植物类物质之外，已经增添了数百种合成毒品，其中许多并不在国际管制之下。药品的非医疗使用也快速增多。	In addition to plant-based substances such as cannabis, cocaine and heroin, hundreds of synthetic drugs have been added, many of which are not under international control. The non-medical use of drugs is also increasing rapidly.	yes
会员国的国内市场每年约有500种新型活性物质。	The domestic markets of Member States are characterized by approximately 500 new active substances per year.	yes
目前其中大多是兴奋剂，其次是合成的大麻素受体激动剂和少量的类阿片。	Most of these are now stimulants, followed by synthetic cannabinoid receptor agonists and, to a lesser extent, opioids.	yes
虽然新型精神活性物质的总体数量已经稳定下来，但比例发生了变化。	While the overall quantity of new psychoactive substances has stabilized, the proportion has changed.	yes
在2014年确定的新型精神活性物质种类总数中，类阿片新型精神活性物质仅占2%,但到2018年，这一数字己上升至9%。	Opioids accounted for only 2 per cent of the total number of new psychoactive substances identified in 2014, but by 2018 that figure had risen to 9 per cent.	yes
类阿片新型精神活性物质中有许多是芬太尼的类似物，其药效和危害已得到证明，在北美导致了过量死亡事件，其他区域也有，但程度较轻。	Many of the new opioid psychoactive substances are analogues of fentanyl, whose efficacy and harm have been demonstrated, leading to overdose deaths in North America and, to a lesser extent, in other regions.	yes
在北美，芬太尼有的用作海洛因和其他毒品（包括可卡因和甲基苯丙胺）的掺杂剂，有的用来制造假冒的药用类阿片。	In North America, fentanyl is used either as an adulterant in heroin and other drugs (including cocaine and methamphetamine) or to manufacture counterfeit pharmaceutical opioids.	yes
一些证据表明，欧洲也有注射新型精神活性物质兴奋剂的现象：一项对欧洲六个城市废弃注射器残留物的研宄发现，许多注射器都沾有产生兴奋作用的新型精神活性物质》	There is some evidence that new psychoactive substance stimulants are also being injected in Europe: a study of discarded syringe residues in six European cities found that many of the syringes were tainted with new psychoactive substances with a euphoric effect.	yes
2新型精神活性物质的使用可能会逐渐牢固存在于弱势群体中	2 Use of new psychoactive substances may gradually become firmly established in vulnerable groups	no
单一种类的新型精神活性物质几乎从未形成大的市场。	There is almost never a large market for a single type of new psychoactive substance.	no
但来自欧洲的证据表明，合成大麻素在无家可归者和监狱囚犯等社会边缘群体中是一个严重的问题。	However, evidence from Europe suggests that synthetic cannabinoids are a serious problem among socially marginalized groups such as the homeless and prison inmates.	no
有22个国家报告了监狱中使用新型精神活性物质的情况，其中大多数国家将合成大麻素确定为主要挑战。	Twenty-two countries reported the use of new psychoactive substances in prisons, with most of them identifying synthetic cannabinoids as the main challenge.	no
对前体化学品的管制迫使制毒者进行创新最常作为前体用来合成苯丙胺、甲基苯丙胺和“摇头丸”等毒品的许多化学品已被置于国际管制之下。	Controls on precursor chemicals have forced drug makers to innovate Many of the chemicals most commonly used as precursors to synthesize drugs such as amphetamines, methamphetamines and "ecstasy" have been placed under international control.	no
贩毒者和制毒者一直在寻找替代品一不仅有管制较松的物质，还有专门为规避管制而设计的化学品，即所谓的“特制前体”。	Drug traffickers and producers are constantly looking for alternatives, not only for less regulated substances, but also for chemicals specifically designed to circumvent controls, so-called "designer precursors".	no
旨在阻止新冠肺炎传播的限制性措施很可能使依赖前体化学品的制毒者受到进一步挤压。	Restrictive measures aimed at stopping the spread of NCP are likely to put a further squeeze on drug producers who rely on precursor chemicals.	no
来自墨西哥的证据表明，这已经成为 现实：据报告，2020年3月，从东亚进口的甲基苯丙胺前体短缺促使墨西哥和美国的甲基苯丙胺价格上涨。	Evidence from Mexico suggests that this has become a reality: in March 2020, a reported shortage of methamphetamine precursors imported from East Asia contributed to an increase in methamphetamine prices in Mexico and the United States.	no
市场瞬息万变	The market is changing rapidly.	no
合成药物在中亚和俄罗斯联邦取代阿片剂	Replacement of opiates by synthetic drugs in Central Asia and the Russian Federation	no
中亚和俄罗斯联邦的阿片剂市场在2008年至2018年期间似乎发生了变化。	The opioid market in Central Asia and the Russian Federation appears to have changed between 2008 and 2018.	no
俄罗斯联邦当局截获的阿片剂数量下降了约80%，同时因使用类阿片而接受治疗的人数大幅减少。	The number of opiates intercepted by the authorities of the Russian Federation declined by about 80 per cent, while the number of people receiving treatment for opioid use decreased significantly.	no
但兴奋剂市场却似乎日渐兴旺。	Yet the doping market seems to be thriving by the day.	no
有证据表明，甲基苯丙胺和各种卡西酮，包括甲氧麻黄酮和 a - 吡咯烷基苯戊酮，现在俄罗斯毒品市场上随处可见。	There is evidence that methamphetamine and various cathinones, including mephedrone and a-pyrrolidinopentanone, are now readily available on the Russian drug market.	no
俄罗斯当局报告称，最近查获的制造各种非法药物的秘密加工点数量急剧上升，在两年内翻了一番多，2018年增至152个加工点。	Russian authorities have reported a sharp rise in the number of recently seized clandestine laboratories manufacturing a wide range of illicit drugs, more than doubling in two years to 152 laboratories in 2018.	no
阿富汗和伊拉克甲基苯丙胺市场增长	Growth of methamphetamine markets in Afghanistan and Iraq	no
早在2012年，对医院、监狱和其他机构人员的调查就已经揭示了甲基苯丙胺在伊拉克的重要性。	As early as 2012, surveys of personnel in hospitals, prisons and other institutions had revealed the importance of methamphetamine in Iraq.	no
结晶甲基苯丙胺已经成为“芬乃他林”和曲马多之外又一种令人担忧的主要药物。	Crystallized methamphetamine has become another major drug of concern in addition to "fenetylline" and tramadol.	no
2015年的一项研宄进一步证实了这些发现，吸毒者表示大麻比“芬乃他林”或甲基苯丙胺更难获得。	These findings were further confirmed by a 2015 study in which drug users reported that marijuana was more difficult to obtain than "fenetylline" or methamphetamine.	no
最近，伊拉克当局发现了多个甲基苯丙胺加工点，麻管局已对伪麻黄碱制剂的大批进口表示关切一甲基苯丙胺加工点将这些制剂用作前体。	Recently, the Iraqi authorities have discovered several methamphetamine laboratories, and the Board has expressed concern about the large-scale importation of pseudoephedrine preparations, which are used as precursors in methamphetamine laboratories.	no
在阿富汗，甲基苯丙胺制造似乎始于2014年。	In Afghanistan, methamphetamine manufacture appears to have begun in 2014.	no
自那时起，甲基苯丙胺的缉获量一直在稳步上升。	Since then, seizures of methamphetamine have been steadily increasing.	no
但2019年上半年的缉获量一^657公斤——与上一年相比大幅骤增。	However, seizures in the first half of 2019 amounted to one ^657 kilograms - a significant jump compared to the previous year.	no
在其他国家大量缉获了据认为源自阿富汗的甲基苯丙胺，这也表明该国的产量正在迅速上升。	Significant seizures of methamphetamine thought to have originated in Afghanistan have been made in other countries, also indicating that production in that country is rising rapidly.	no
政策变化和变化趋势	Policy changes and trends	yes
非医疗使用大麻合法化的法域大多有大麻使用增多的趋势	Most jurisdictions that have legalized the non-medical use of cannabis have shown a trend of increased cannabis use	yes
加拿大、乌拉圭和美国的11个法域允许制造大麻产品供非医疗使用。	Eleven jurisdictions in Canada, Uruguay and the United States allow the manufacture of cannabis products for non-medical use.	yes
在其中多数法域，大麻使用自合法化以来有所增多，尽管在其他未将非医疗使用大麻合法化的法域也观察到了同样的趋势。	In most of those jurisdictions, cannabis use has increased since legalization, although the same trend has been observed in other jurisdictions that have not legalized the non-medical use of cannabis.	yes
在美国最早通过立法的两个州科罗拉多州和华盛顿州，成年人非医疗使用大麻的情况增加，特别是过去一个月以及每天或几乎每天使用的情况增多，自2012年起便已超过了全国平均水平。	In Colorado and Washington, two of the first states in the U.S. to pass legislation, non-medical use of marijuana by adults has increased, especially in the past month and on a daily or near-daily basis, and has exceeded the national average since 2012.	yes
所有指标都显示，自2011年以来，乌拉圭的大麻使用情况有所增加，上月使用情况几乎翻了一番。	All indicators show an increase in cannabis use in Uruguay since 2011, with use almost doubling in the last month.	yes
这表明增加的主要原因是经常和频繁使用大麻。	This suggests that the main reason for the increase is the regular and frequent use of marijuana.	yes
加拿大的短期数据也表明，2018年至2019年合法市场扩大的同时，使用量也在增加。	Short-term data from Canada also suggests that the expansion of the legal market from 2018 to 2019 was accompanied by an increase in usage.	yes
然而，2019年仍有40%的大麻使用者靠非法来源获得某些产品。	However, 40% of marijuana users still rely on illegal sources to obtain certain products in 2019.	yes
全球大麻药草缉获量暴跌的背后原因是大麻合法化？	Marijuana Legalization Behind Plummeting Global Cannabis Herb Seizures?	yes
2018年，全球大麻药草缉获量降至20年来的最低水平，这是因为北美的缉获量下降，在过去10年中下降了 84%。	In 2018, global cannabis herb seizures fell to their lowest level in 20 years, driven by declining seizures in North America, which have fallen by 84 per cent over the past 10 years.	no
相比之下，同期世界其他地区的缉获量几乎翻了一番。缉获的模式表明，旨在放开大麻市场的政策在下降中发挥了关键作用。	In contrast, seizures in the rest of the world almost doubled over the same period. The pattern of seizures suggests that policies aimed at liberalizing cannabis markets have played a key role in the decline.	no
对新型精神活性物质的监管似乎有遏制作用在国内对新型精神活性物质的监管效果仍然很难评估。	Regulation of new psychoactive substances appears to have a deterrent effect The effectiveness of regulation of new psychoactive substances in the country remains difficult to assess.	no
一些对新型精神活性物质采用不同监管制度的国家显示出不同的新型精神活性物质使用流行率。	A number of countries with different regulatory regimes for new psychoactive substances show different prevalence rates of new psychoactive substance use.	no
在另一些国家，通过国内立法后，新型精神活性物质使用情况有所减少。	In other countries, the adoption of domestic legislation has led to a decrease in the use of new psychoactive substances.	no
弱势群体面临合法和非法毒品市场的伤害用于疼痛管理和姑息治疗的药用类阿片主要在高收入国家提供止痛药在各区域分布不均。	Vulnerable groups face harm from licit and illicit drug markets Pharmaceutical opioids for pain management and palliative care are mainly available in high-income countries Analgesics are unevenly distributed across regions.	no
2018年，所有可供医疗消费的药用类阿片中，90%以上在高收入国家。	In 2018, more than 90% of all medicinal opioids available for medical consumption were in high-income countries.	no
大约50%在北美，40%在欧洲，还有2%在大洋洲。	About 50% are in North America, 40% in Europe, and 2% in Oceania.	no
这些国家的人口约占全球人口的12%。	These countries are home to about 12% of the global population.	no
据估计，低收入和中等收入国家的人口占全球人口的88%,但消费的药用类阿片却不到10%。	It is estimated that low- and middle-income countries account for 88 per cent of the global population but consume less than 10 per cent of pharmaceutical opioids.	no
获取药用类阿片的障碍与许多因素有关，包括立法、文化、卫生系统和处方做法。	Barriers to accessing pharmaceutical opioids are related to many factors, including legislation, culture, health systems and prescribing practices.	no
较贫穷的人患吸毒病症的风险更大2018年约有3,560万人患有吸毒病症。	Poorer people are at greater risk of developing a drug use disorder In 2018 about 35.6 million people suffered from a drug use disorder.	no
贫困、有限的教育和社会边缘化可能会增加吸毒病症风险，并加剧其后果。高收入国家的研宄证实了这一点，在这些研究中，个人不利的社会经济轨迹一不仅仅是他们在某一时间点的状况一也与吸毒病症风险有关。	Poverty, limited education and social marginalization may increase the risk of drug use disorders and exacerbate their consequences. This is confirmed by researchers in high-income countries, where individuals' unfavourable socio-economic trajectories, not only their situation at a given point in time, are also associated with the risk of drug use disorders.	no
吸毒病症还会加深社会经济劣势，进一步增加失业、贫困和无家可归的风险，从而助长劣势的恶性循环。这些结果也可能与刑事司法系统内的侮辱性态度和后果有关。	Drug use disorders can also deepen socio-economic disadvantage, further increasing the risk of unemployment, poverty and homelessness, thus contributing to a vicious cycle of disadvantage. These outcomes may also be linked to stigmatizing attitudes and consequences within the criminal justice system.	no
妇女、少数民族和移民、性取向多样化群体、因武装冲突或灾难而流离失所的人以及农村环境中的人也可能受到吸毒病症的过重影响，或者在获得治疗服务方面遇到问题。	Women, ethnic minorities and migrants, sexually diverse groups, persons displaced by armed conflict or disaster and persons in rural settings may also be disproportionately affected by drug use disorders or experience problems in accessing treatment services.	no
根据估计因残疾和过早死亡而损失的健康寿命年数的残疾调整寿命年（DALY)指标，在过去10年中，有害的吸毒对范围更广的社会影响加重。	According to the Disability-Adjusted Life Years (DALY) indicator, which estimates the number of healthy life years lost due to disability and premature death, the impact of harmful drug use on the wider society has increased over the past 10 years.	no
2007年至2018年间，归因于吸毒的全球残疾调整寿命年数增加了 17%。	Between 2007 and 2018, the number of global disability-adjusted life years attributable to drug use increased by 17 per cent.	no
注射吸毒者中常见的未经治疗的丙型肝炎导致的肝癌的相关残疾调整寿命年数增幅特别高——达到40%。	The increase in DALYs associated with hepatocellular carcinoma due to untreated hepatitis C, which is common among injecting drug users, was particularly high - up to 40%.	no
毒品和暴力之间的关系错综复杂很难确定精神活性物质的使用和暴力之间的所有因果关系。	The relationship between drugs and violence is complex and it is difficult to establish all the causal links between the use of psychoactive substances and violence.	no
全球范围的有限数据表明，迷醉可能是杀人的一个重要因素。	The limited data available globally suggests that intoxication may be an important factor in homicide.	no
但在暴力事件中，酒精的作用似乎比毒品更大。	But alcohol seems to play a bigger role in violence than drugs.	no
虽然吸毒可能会导致犯罪，但在某些情况下，这种联系可以部分归因于多种中介因素，如社会经济劣势以及由个人风险、家庭环境和同龄人影响造成的其他类型的逆境。	While drug use may lead to offending, in some cases the link can be partially attributed to multiple mediating factors, such as socio-economic disadvantage and other types of adversity caused by personal risk, family circumstances and peer influence.	no
贩毒和暴力之间的联系是多方面的。	The links between drug trafficking and violence are manifold.	no
如果已有稳定的犯罪结构，包括国际贩毒在内的大规模有组织犯罪活动有可能在无暴力的情况下实施。	Large-scale organized criminal activities, including international drug trafficking, are likely to be committed without violence if stable criminal structures are in place.	no
短期内，暴力的存在和程度与其说取决于贩运的数量，不如说取决于造成有组织犯罪集团之间力量平衡不稳定的某些变化，例如非法市场规模的变化，知名罪犯的死亡或监禁，以及使一个集团弱于另一个集团的执法措施。	In the short term, the existence and extent of violence depends less on the volume of trafficking than on certain changes that create an unstable balance of power between organized criminal groups, such as changes in the size of the illicit market, the death or imprisonment of high-profile offenders, and law enforcement measures that make one group weaker than another.	no
最新趋势	Latest trends	yes
吸毒大麻是最常用的物质，类阿片危害最大	Addiction Marijuana is the most commonly used substance, opioids most harmful	yes
据估计，2018年使用大麻的有 1.92 亿人，使之成为全球使用最多的毒品。	An estimated 192 million people used marijuana in 2018, making it the most used drug in the world.	yes
相比之下，2018年使用类阿片的有5,800万人。	In comparison, 58 million people used opioids in 2018.	yes
但阿片类药物的相关危害却因使用者较少而受到忽视。	However, the harms associated with opioids have been overlooked because of the low number of users.	yes
在2017年与吸毒病症有关的估计167,000例死亡中，有66%是这类物质造成的，在据信为吸毒导致的残疾或过早死亡而损失的2,100万年寿命中，有50%是这类物质造成的。	Such substances were responsible for 66 percent of the estimated 167,000 deaths related to drug use disorders in 2017, and 50 percent of the 21 million years of life believed to have been lost to disability or premature death due to drug use.	yes
合成类阿片的非医疗使用加剧了公共卫生危机	Non-medical use of synthetic opioids exacerbates public health crisis	yes
在西非、中部非洲和北非，加剧类阿片危机的是曲马多；在北美则是芬太尼。这两个区域在经济、人口统计数据或一般吸毒模式方面几乎没有共同点，但都在奋力抗击由容易获得且生产成本低的物质助长的类阿片危机。	In West, Central and North Africa, it is tramadol that fuels the opioid crisis; in North America, it is fentanyl. The two regions have little in common in terms of economies, demographics or general patterns of drug use, but both are struggling to combat the opioid crisis, which is fuelled by substances that are readily available and cheap to produce.	yes
在北美，芬太尼等合成类阿片的使用导致了20年来类阿片过量致死人数增加。	In North America, the use of synthetic opioids such as fentanyl has led to a 20-year increase in opioid overdose deaths.	yes
2018年，在美国登记的67,367例过量死亡中，有三分之二涉及芬太尼。	In 2018, two-thirds of the 67,367 overdose deaths registered in the U.S. involved fentanyl.	yes
加拿大也报告了类似的结果，只是数字较低。	Canada reported similar results, only in lower numbers.	no
芬太尼导致过量死亡的部分原因是非法药物市场上的芬太尼药效不可预测。	Fentanyl causes overdose deaths in part because of the unpredictable potency of fentanyl on the illicit drug market.	no
在西非、中部非洲和北非，非医疗用途曲马多的市场已有大幅增长。	In West, Central and North Africa, the market for non-medical Tramadol has grown significantly.	no
在该区域，接受治疗的曲马多使用病症患者越来越多。	An increasing number of patients with Tramadol Use Disorder are being treated in the region.	no
2017年，全球截获的曲马多数量显著增加，达到125吨以上的峰值。	In 2017, global interceptions of tramadol increased significantly, peaking at more than 125 tons.	no
但2018年，在印度通过一项监管曲马多的新法律之后，全球缉获量降至32吨。	In 2018, however, global seizures fell to 32 tons after India passed a new law regulating tramadol.	no
促成这两地危机的是制造简单和生产成本低，此外还有对曲马多和许多芬太尼类似物或其前体缺乏国际监管。	Contributing to the crises in both places were the simplicity of manufacture and the low cost of production, in addition to the lack of international regulation of tramadol and many fentanyl analogues or their precursors.	no
使这两地危机恶化的是这些物质在药品市场和非法市场上都有供应，因而更加难以发现和防止其滥用。	Exacerbating the crisis in both places is the fact that these substances are available on both the pharmaceutical and illicit markets, making it more difficult to detect and prevent their abuse.	no
兴奋剂使用不断增多	Doping is on the rise	no
兴奋剂领域以可卡因和甲基苯丙胺为主，这两种物质在其主要市场的使用量都在上升。	The area of stimulants is dominated by cocaine and methamphetamine, both of which are increasing in use in their major markets.	no
2018年使用可卡因的约有1,900万人，因为可卡因在北美和西欧颇为流行。	About 19 million people used cocaine in 2018, as cocaine is quite popular in North America and Western Europe.	no
同年使用苯丙胺的约有2,700万人，其中甲基苯丙胺是东南亚和北美使用最多的苯丙胺类兴奋剂。	Approximately 27 million people used amphetamines in the same year, with methamphetamine being the most used amphetamine-type stimulant in South-East Asia and North America.	no
根据所掌握的多数指标，20年来这两个区域甲基苯丙胺的使用一直在扩大。	According to most indicators available, methamphetamine use has been expanding in both regions for 20 years.	no
在一些市场上，可卡因和甲基苯丙胺可以共存，有时是相互替代，这样一种药物的使用量上升时另一种药物的使用量就下降，有时是同时增加和减少以满足同一市场的需求。	In some markets, cocaine and methamphetamine can coexist, sometimes substituting for each other so that the use of one drug rises when the use of the other falls, and sometimes increasing and decreasing at the same time to meet demand in the same market.	no
新冠肺炎使注射吸毒者的风险增高	New Crown Pneumonia Puts Injecting Drug Users at Increased Risk	no
据估计，2018年注射吸毒的约有1,130万人，全球艾滋病毒感染约有10%是注射吸毒造成的。	It is estimated that about 11.3 million people injected drugs in 2018 and that about 10 percent of global HIV infections are caused by injecting drug use.	no
注射吸毒者感染艾滋病毒的超过100万人，患丙型肝炎的有550万人。	More than 1 million injecting drug users are infected with HIV, and 5.5 million people have hepatitis C.	no
2017年，因吸毒死亡的约有 58.5万人，其中一半死于丙型肝炎引起的肝病，而注射吸毒者的丙型肝炎大多仍未得到治疗。	In 2017, there were about 585,000 deaths due to drug use, half of which were due to liver disease caused by hepatitis C, which remains largely untreated in injecting drug users.	no
5 新冠肺炎限制措施造成的类阿片短缺可能导致使用者代之以酒精或苯二氮类药物等更容易获得的物质，或者将类阿片与合成药物混合。	5 Shortages of opioids resulting from the NCRP restrictions may lead users to substitute more readily available substances, such as alcohol or benzodiazepines, or to mix opioids with synthetic drugs.	no

欧盟峰会为难民政策争论，欧盟官员：接收过程步步瓶颈-中新网	EU summit argues over refugee policy, EU official: reception process bottlenecks at every step - CNN.com	yes
欧盟峰会为难民政策争吵不休，欧盟官员：接收过程每一步都存在瓶颈	EU summit squabbles over refugee policy, EU official: bottlenecks at every step of reception process	yes
【环球时报驻比利时特派记者 牛瑞飞】据法新社2月10日报道，在当天最新的一次欧盟峰会上，欧盟委员会主席冯德莱恩表示，欧盟领导人同意就非法移民问题出台更严格的政策，以此更易于驱逐非法移民。	[Global Times in Belgium Special Correspondent Niu Ruifei] According to AFP on February 10, at the latest EU summit on the same day, European Commission President von der Leyen said that EU leaders agreed to introduce a stricter policy on illegal immigration as a way to make it easier to deport illegal immigrants.	yes
据报道，欧盟此举是对欧洲日益增长的非法移民问题关注的回应，如今，欧盟的核心问题在于，最终能被遣返的非法移民人数很少。	The move by the EU is reportedly a response to growing concerns about illegal immigration in Europe, which today is centered on the small number of illegal immigrants who can ultimately be repatriated.	yes
根据峰会文件，欧盟领导人呼吁委员会“立即调动大量欧盟资金”，以基础设施和监视等手段加强外部边界。	According to the summit document, EU leaders called on the Commission to "immediately mobilize substantial EU funds" to strengthen the external borders with infrastructure and surveillance.	yes
然而，欧盟与各成员国就围栏费用支付等问题争吵不休。	However, the EU is at loggerheads with member states over issues such as payment for the fence.	yes
冯德莱恩一再表示，欧盟资金不会支付相关费用。	Von der Leyen has repeatedly said that EU funds will not cover the costs involved.	yes
但一些成员国的外交官员称，如果欧盟能分担外部边界沿线安装摄像头、瞭望塔和其他基础设施的部分，这将给各国腾出国家预算从而加快建设进程。	But diplomatic officials from some member states say that if the EU were to share the portion of the installation of cameras, watchtowers and other infrastructure along the external borders, it would free up national budgets for countries to speed up the construction process.	yes
欧洲Euractiv网站称，欧盟官员承认，难民接收过程每一步都存在瓶颈，有限的接收能力和成员国不堪重负的移民当局无法阻止难民在欧盟各国提交“无数”庇护申请，欧盟的难民接收系统处于近乎“永久性的危机”中。	According to Europe's Euractiv website, EU officials have acknowledged that there are bottlenecks at every step of the refugee reception process, and that the EU's refugee reception system is in a near "permanent crisis" as limited reception capacity and overburdened migration authorities in member states are unable to prevent refugees from submitting "countless" asylum applications across the EU. permanent crisis".	yes
据欧盟委员会估计，欧盟的申根国家去年收到超92万份庇护申请，比前一年增加近半。	The European Commission estimates that the EU's Schengen states received more than 920,000 asylum applications last year, an increase of nearly half from the previous year.	yes
与此同时，欧盟去年记录到超 33万次非法入境。	Meanwhile, the EU recorded more than 330,000 illegal entries last year.	no
在该背景下，此次峰会还就一项“原则”达成协议，即欧盟国家可根据另一个成员国的法院判决将非法移民遣返回国。	In this context, the summit also agreed on the "principle" that EU countries can return illegal immigrants to their home countries on the basis of a court decision in another member state.	no
此外，报道称，欧盟领导人还同意“增加对安全国家概念的使用”，这将为欧盟制定共同清单开辟道路。	In addition, EU leaders agreed to "increase the use of the concept of the security state," which would open the way for the EU to develop a common list, according to the report.	no

首批个人养老金理财产品开售	First personal pension financial products go on sale	yes
家机构的7只产品可选 最短可只持有360天	7 products from 7 institutions to choose from Minimum holding time of 360 days only	yes
个人养老金理财产品终于上线了。	Personal pension financial products have finally gone live.	yes
2月10日，中国理财网发布首批个人养老金理财产品名单，工银理财、农银理财和中邮理财的7只个人养老金理财产品正式发售。	On February 10, China Wealth Management released the list of the first batch of personal pension financial products, and seven personal pension financial products from ICBC Wealth Management, Agricultural Bank of China Wealth Management and China Post Wealth Management were officially put on sale.	yes
至此，个人养老金账户的“货架”终于集齐个人养老金储蓄、个人养老金理财、个人养老金保险、个人养老金公募基金四类产品。	So far, the personal pension account "shelf" finally gathered personal pension savings, personal pension financial management, personal pension insurance, personal pension public fund four types of products.	yes

北京青年报记者看到，5只新发产品中有4只来自工银理财，全部是固定收益类产品，最短持有期限分别为365天、540天、720天和1080天，对应的业绩比较基准(年化)分别为3.70 % - 4.20 % 、 4.10 % - 4.60 % 、 4.40 % - 4.90 % 、 5.25 % - 5.75 % 。	The Beijing Youth Daily reporter saw that four of the five newly issued products were from ICBC Wealth Management, all of which were fixed-income products, with minimum holding periods of 365 days, 540 days, 720 days and 1080 days, and corresponding performance comparison benchmarks (annualized) of 3.70% - 4.20%, 4.10% - 4.60%, 4.40% - 4.90%, 5.25% - 5.75%. The benchmarks are 3.70% - 4.20%, 4.10% - 4.60%, 4.40% - 4.90%, 5.25% - 5.75%.	yes
剩余一只新发产品是“邮银财富添颐·鸿锦最短持有1095 天 1 号 ” ， 也是固定收益类产品，2月10日开始募集，2月19日结束募集，风险等级为二级。	The remaining new product is "Postbank Wealth Tiyi-Hong Jin Minimum Holding Days 1,095 No. 1", which is also a fixed-income product, with the fund-raising process starting on February 10th and ending on February 19th, and with a risk rating of Level II.	yes
两只存续产品中，一只是农银理财“农银同心·灵动”360天科技创新人民币理财产品，投资性质为混合类，风险等级为三级。	Of the two surviving products, one is the "Agribank Concentric - Lingdang" 360-day technological innovation RMB financial product of Agribank Wealth Management, which is of mixed nature and has a risk level of Grade 3.	yes
另一只存续产品是“邮银财富添颐·鸿锦最短持有365 天 1 号 ” ， 固定收益类型，去年12月30日开始募集，今年1月4日正式运作，2月8日的累计净值为1.0011。	The other surviving product is "Postbank Wealth Tiyi-Hong Jin Minimum Holding 365 Days No. 1", fixed-income type, which was launched on December 30 last year and formally operated on January 4 this year, with a cumulative net value of 1.0011 on February 8, the product has been in the market for a long time and is expected to be launched in the near future.	no
根据《国务院办公厅关于推动个人养老金发展的意见 》 ， 个人养老金资金账户资金可投资的金融产品包括银行理财、储蓄存款、商业养老保险、公募基金等。	According to the Opinions of the General Office of the State Council on Promoting the Development of Individual Pensions, the financial products in which funds in individual pension accounts can be invested include bank wealth management, savings deposits, commercial pension insurance and public funds.	no
首批个人养老金理财产品发售，标志着个人养老金投资者可正式通过个人养老金资金账户购买理财产品。	The first batch of personal pension financial products are put on sale, marking the fact that personal pension investors can formally purchase financial products through their personal pension fund accounts.	no
去年11月银保监会制定了《商业银行和理财公司个人养老金业务管理暂行办法 》 。	In November last year, the CBIRC formulated the Interim Measures for the Administration of Personal Pension Businesses of Commercial Banks and Wealth Management Companies.	no
《办法》规定，参加人可以通过个人养老金资金账户购买个人养老储蓄、个人养老金理财产品、个人养老金保险产品、个人养老金公募基金产品等个人养老金产品。	The Measures provide that participants may purchase personal pension products such as personal pension savings, personal pension financial products, personal pension insurance products and personal pension public fund products through their personal pension fund accounts.	no
随后，人社部、财政部、国家税务总局三部门发布通知，明确个人养老金制度在北京、天津，以及河北石家庄、雄安新区，山西晋城市等36个先行城市和地区启动实施。	Subsequently, the Ministry of Human Resources and Social Security, the Ministry of Finance and the State Administration of Taxation issued a notice specifying that the personal pension system was launched in Beijing and Tianjin, as well as 36 pioneer cities and regions such as Shijiazhuang and Xiong'an New Area in Hebei and Jincheng City in Shanxi.	no
截至2022年底，个人养老金参加人数1954万人，缴费人数613万人，总缴费金额142亿元。	By the end of 2022, there were 19.54 million individual pension participants, 6.13 million contributors, and total contributions of $14.2 billion.	no
此前，参与试点的银行只上架了个人养老储蓄、个人养老金保险产品和个人养老金公募基金三类产品。	Previously, the banks participating in the pilot program only had three types of products on their shelves: personal pension savings, personal pension insurance products and personal pension public funds.	no
如今，个人养老金理财产品也聚齐之后，投资者该如何选择？	Now, after the personal pension financial products are also gathered, how should investors choose?	no
交银理财产品研发部专家表示，相比其他个人养老金产品，试点阶段的养老理财产品和个人养老金理财产品均具有三方面的特点。	Experts from the R&D department of CBI's financial products said that compared to other personal pension products, both the pilot stage pension financial products and personal pension financial products are characterized by three aspects.	no
一是稳健性，风险管理机制更加健全，投资策略和理念更为稳健，并实施非母行第三方独立托管。	The first is robustness, with a more robust risk management mechanism, more robust investment strategies and philosophies, and the implementation of independent third-party custodianship by a non-parent bank.	no
二是长期性，试点阶段养老理财产品的期限都在5年及以上，下一步发行的个人养老金理财产品，最短持有期原则上为1年，鼓励持有3年以上。	Second, long-term, the pilot phase of the pension financial products are five years and above, the next step in the issuance of personal pension financial products, the shortest holding period is in principle one year, encouraged to hold more than three years.	no
三是普惠性，产品购买门槛低，起购点一般为1元，有的低至0.01元，产品的托管费、管理费等费率更加优惠。	The third is universality, the product purchase threshold is low, the starting point is generally 1 yuan, some as low as 0.01 yuan, the product's custodian fee, management fee and other rates are more favorable.	no
专业人士指出，投资者要根据产品特点和自己的风险承受能力进行选择。	Professionals pointed out that investors should choose according to the characteristics of the product and their own risk tolerance.	no
个人养老金储蓄具有期限较长、利率较高、安全性高的特点，适合风险承受能力弱的人群；个人养老金保险产品重在保障，比较适合无法承担投资风险，可以接受稳定收益的人群；而个人养老金理财产品和公募基金产品不保本也不保收益，有一定投资风险，但预期收益较高，适合具备一定的金融知识、风险承担能力较高的人群。	Personal pension savings have the characteristics of longer term, higher interest rate and high security, which are suitable for people with weak risk-tolerance ability; personal pension insurance products emphasize on protection, which are more suitable for people who can't bear the investment risk and can accept the stable income; and personal pension financial products and public fund products don't guarantee the capital or the income, which have a certain investment risk, but the expected income is higher, which is suitable for people who have a certain degree of financial knowledge and higher risk-tolerance ability. They have certain investment risks but higher expected returns, and are suitable for people with certain financial knowledge and higher risk-bearing ability.	no

".	yes

种植牙齿指的是一种以植入骨组织内的下部结构为基础来支持、固位上部牙修复体的缺牙修复方式。	Dental implants refer to a type of missing tooth restoration that is based on a lower structure implanted into the bone tissue to support and retain the upper dental restoration.	yes
记者从郑州大学第一附属医院了解到，以单颗常规种植为例，从种植到最后修复，价格大概要一万六七千元左右。	The reporter learned from the First Affiliated Hospital of Zhengzhou University that the price of a single conventional implant, for example, from the implant to the final restoration, is about sixteen or seven thousand dollars.	yes

The ECHI report analyzes the importance of quality content, the "new variable" in the current e-commerce industry, from the data dimension, and evaluates the content ecology of 27 mainstream e-commerce platforms in China.	no
根据上述报告的电商行业内容生态健康指数排名，抖音电商、快手、淘宝、拼多多、京东位居前五。	According to the e-commerce industry's content ecological health index ranking in the above report, Jitterbug e-commerce, Shutterbug, Taobao, Pinduoduo, and Jingdong are in the top five.	no
报告认为，电商行业内容生态是一个综合性概念，是将电商与内容进行整合，但并非所有内容都可与电商整合，好的PGC(专业生产内容)与UGC(用户原创内容)才是与电商进行整合的优质载体，内容平台价值越高，消费与推广的场景也就越来越丰富，电商植入的可能性也就越高，商业价值也就越强，这种公共领域和私人领域逐步集成分布的电商内容生产和内容消费的比例也就会越高。	The report argues that the content ecology of the e-commerce industry is a comprehensive concept that integrates e-commerce with content, but not all content can be integrated with e-commerce, and that good PGC (professionally produced content) and UGC (user-originated content) are the high-quality carriers of integration with e-commerce, and the higher the value of the content platforms, the richer the scenarios of consumption and promotion, and the higher the possibilities of e-commerce implantation. The stronger the commercial value, the higher the proportion of e-commerce content production and content consumption distributed by this gradual integration of the public and private spheres.	no
现场，北京师范大学新闻传播学院教授、中国传媒经济与管理专业委员会理事长喻国明对《报告》做了分析解读。	On the scene, Yu Guoming, a professor at the School of Journalism and Communication of Beijing Normal University and chairman of the China Media Economics and Management Professional Committee, analyzed and interpreted the Report.	no

另一个是从外部生态看，要实现内容电商行业的健康发展和外部环境的价值协同与共创。	The other is from the external ecological point of view, to realize the healthy development of the content e-commerce industry and the external environment of value synergy and co-creation.	no

推进中国式现代化涉及经济、政治、文化、社会、生态文明等各个领域，关系治党治国治军、内政外交国防等方方面面，既要做好系统谋划，又要勇于改革创新，不断实现整体推进。	Promoting Chinese-style modernization involves various fields such as economy, politics, culture, society and ecological civilization, and is related to all aspects of the governance of the Party, the State, the military, internal affairs, diplomacy and national defense, so it is necessary to do a good job of systematic planning, but also the courage to reform and innovation, and to continuously realize the overall advancement.	yes
进行顶层设计，需要深刻洞察世界发展大势，准确把握人民群众的共同愿望，深入探索经济社会发展规律，使制定的规划和政策体系体现时代性、把握规律性、富于创造性，做到远近结合、上下贯通、内容协调。	To carry out top-level design, it is necessary to gain a deep insight into the general trend of world development, accurately grasp the common aspirations of the people, and explore in depth the laws of economic and social development, so that the planning and policy system formulated reflects the times, grasps the regularities, and is rich in creativity, and achieves a combination of near and far, up and down, and harmonization of content.	yes
推进中国式现代化是一个探索性事业，还有许多未知领域，需要在实践中去大胆探索，通过改革创新来推动事业发展，决不能刻舟求剑、守株待兔。	Promoting Chinese-style modernization is an exploratory undertaking, and there are still many uncharted territories that need to be boldly explored in practice, and the undertaking should be promoted through reform and innovation, and should never be carved up or guarded.	yes
战略问题是一个政党、一个国家的根本性问题。	Strategic issues are fundamental to a political party and a country.	yes
推进中国式现代化，要增强战略的前瞻性，以科学的战略预见未来、引领未来；要增强战略的全局性，着眼于解决事关党和国家事业兴衰成败、牵一发而动全身的重大问题；要增强战略的稳定性，战略一经形成，就要长期坚持、一抓到底、善作善成。	To promote Chinese-style modernization, it is necessary to enhance the foresight of the strategy, to foresee the future and lead the future with a scientific strategy; to enhance the overall situation of the strategy, focusing on solving the major problems that have a bearing on the success or failure of the Party and the country's cause, and affecting the whole body in one hair; to enhance the stability of the strategy, and to adhere to the strategy for a long period of time, to grasp it to the end, and to achieve good results once the strategy has been formed.	yes
要科学把握战略和策略的辩证统一关系，把战略的原则性和策略的灵活性有机结合起来，灵活机动、随机应变、临机决断，在因地制宜、因势而动、顺势而为中把握战略主动。	We should scientifically grasp the dialectical and unified relationship between strategy and tactics, organically combine the principle of strategy and the flexibility of tactics, be flexible, adaptive and decisive, and seize the strategic initiative by adapting to local conditions, moving in response to the situation and acting in accordance with the situation.	no
中华民族是守正创新的民族。	The Chinese nation is a nation of righteousness and innovation.	no
处理好守正与创新的关系，既要守好中国式现代化的本和源、根和魂，毫不动摇坚持中国式现代化的中国特色、本质要求、重大原则，确保中国式现代化的正确方向，又要把创新摆在国家发展全局的突出位置，顺应时代发展要求，着眼于解决重大理论和实践问题，积极识变应变求变，大力推进改革创新，不断塑造发展新动能新优势，充分激发全社会创造活力。	In order to handle the relationship between keeping the right and innovation well, it is necessary not only to keep the origin, root and soul of Chinese-style modernization, and unswervingly adhere to the Chinese characteristics, essential requirements and major principles of Chinese-style modernization, so as to ensure that Chinese-style modernization is in the right direction, but also to place innovation in a prominent position in the overall situation of the country's development, conform to the requirements of the times, focus on solving major theoretical and practical problems, actively recognize and respond to changes, and vigorously promote reform and innovation, and constantly shape new dynamics and new advantages for development to fully stimulate the creative vitality of the whole society. We should promote reform and innovation, continuously shape new momentum and new advantages for development, and fully stimulate the creative energies of society as a whole.	no
效率是公平的重要基础，公平是效率的有力保证。	Efficiency is an important foundation for fairness, and fairness is a strong guarantee of efficiency.	no

（德国之声中文网）拜登政府本周五（2月10日）将6个与疑似参与间谍气球计划的中国实体列入黑名单。	(Deutsche Welle Chinese) The Biden administration this Friday (Feb. 10) blacklisted six Chinese entities associated with a suspected spy balloon program.	yes
美国商务部表示，这5家中国公司及1家研究机构帮助中国军队现代化，尤其是航空航天项目，包括飞艇和飞机。	The U.S. Department of Commerce said the five Chinese companies and a research institute help modernize China's military, particularly its aerospace programs, including blimps and aircraft.	yes
被列入黑名单的公司很难获得美国的技术出口。	Blacklisted companies have difficulty obtaining U.S. technology exports.	yes
名单被称为“实体名单”（entity list），入列的公司除非获得美国商务部的特别出口许可证，否则将无法向美国供应商购买技术或商品。	The list is known as the "entity list," and companies on it are unable to purchase technology or goods from U.S. suppliers unless they receive a special export license from the U.S. Department of Commerce.	yes
被列入黑名单的公司是：北京南江空天科技股份有限公司、中国电子科技集团第四十八研究所、东莞凌空遥感科技有限公司、鹰门航空科技集团有限公司、广州天海翔航空科技有限公司和山西鹰门航空科技集团有限公司。	The blacklisted companies are: Beijing Nanjiang Air & Space Technology Co., Ltd, China Electronics Technology Group Forty-eighth Research Institute, Dongguan Lingkong Remote Sensing Technology Co., Ltd, Eagle Gate Aeronautical Science & Technology Group Co., Ltd, Guangzhou Tianhaixiang Aeronautical Science & Technology Co., Ltd and Shanxi Eagle Gate Aeronautical Science & Technology Group Co.	yes
在此之前，白宫表示考虑做出更广泛措施，“揭露和处理”中国威胁美国国家安全的更大规模监控活动。	This comes after the White House said it was considering broader measures to "expose and address" China's larger surveillance activities that threaten U.S. national security.	yes
气球事件引发中美之间进一步紧张，美国国务卿布林肯取消了访问中国的行程。	The balloon incident triggered further tensions between the U.S. and China, and U.S. Secretary of State Abraham Blinken canceled his visit to China.	yes
美国2月4日击落气球，中国政府向美国驻华使馆提出严正交涉，批评美国严重冲击和损害双方稳定中美关系的努力和进程。	In response to the shooting down of the balloon by the United States on 4 February, the Chinese Government lodged solemn representations with the United States Embassy in Beijing, criticizing the United States for seriously impacting on and undermining the efforts and processes of both sides to stabilize China-United States relations.	yes
从现有残骸证据及中国军方的采购平台资讯，美国政府得出结论，认为该气球的制造厂商“跟中国解放军有直接关系”，而且是中国军方批准的供应商。	From the available evidence of wreckage and information on the Chinese military's procurement platform, the United States Government concluded that the balloon's manufacturer had a "direct relationship with the Chinese People's Liberation Army" and was an approved supplier to the Chinese military.	yes
中国外交部发言人毛宁在周五的新闻发布会上表示，关于一只中国无人民用飞艇因不可抗力误入美国领空的意外事件，中方已经多次说明情况、阐明立场。	Chinese Foreign Ministry spokesman Mao Ning said at a news conference on Friday that China has repeatedly explained the situation and clarified its position on the accidental incident of a Chinese unmanned civilian blimp that mistakenly entered U.S. airspace due to force majeure.	yes

60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most destructive earthquake to hit the world in 60 years	no
智利大地震（1960年）	Great Chilean Earthquake (1960)	no
当地时间1960年5月22日下午3点11分，智利瓦尔迪维亚发生人类史上观测记录到的规模最大的地震，地震矩规模为9.5。	On May 22, 1960, at 3:11 p.m. local time, the largest earthquake ever observed and recorded in human history occurred in Valdivia, Chile, with a seismic moment magnitude of 9.5	no
短短十分钟内，瓦尔迪维亚整座城市变为废墟。	In just ten minutes, the entire city of Valdivia was reduced to rubble.	no
地震之后引发的巨大海啸袭击到智利海岸线，掀起浪高高度是25米高的巨大海啸。	A huge tsunami triggered by the earthquake hit the Chilean coastline, creating a massive wave height of 25 meters.	no
海啸波及到遥远的日本、菲律宾。	The tsunami reached as far away as Japan and the Philippines.	no
如此范围的灾难所造成的罹难人数以及经济损失无法精确得知。	The number of victims and the economic damage caused by a disaster of this magnitude cannot be known with precision.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most destructive earthquake to hit the world in 60 years	no
阿拉斯加大地震（1964年）	Great Alaskan Earthquake (1964)	no
1964年3月27日是一个星期五，也是是耶稣受难日。	March 27, 1964 was a Friday and was also Good Friday.	no
这一天美国阿拉斯加发生北美洲历史上最大的地震，矩震级达到9.2。	On this day the largest earthquake in the history of North America occurred in Alaska, USA, with a moment magnitude of 9.2.	no
直到2006年，阿拉斯加大地震仍然是有纪录以来世界第三大地震。	Until 2006, the Great Alaska Earthquake remained the third largest earthquake in the world on record.	no
地震发生时，太平洋板块和北美洲板块之间的一个断层在威廉王子湾接近学院峡湾的地方断裂。	The earthquake occurred when a fault between the Pacific and North American plates broke in Prince William Sound near College Gap.	no
在大部分的地区这场地震持续了3分钟到5分钟。	The quake lasted between three and five minutes in most areas.	no
海床位移引发了巨大的海啸，高度为67米。	Displacement of the seabed triggered a huge tsunami with a height of 67 meters.	no
由于当天是假日，所以学校和许多企业都关闭了。	Since it was a holiday, schools and many businesses were closed.	no
这场大地震最后导致了139人罹难。	The earthquake ended up killing 139 people.	no
其中9人直接死于地震，其他130人死于地震引发的海啸。	Nine of them died as a direct result of the earthquake, while 130 others died as a result of the tsunami triggered by the earthquake.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most destructive earthquake to hit the world in 60 years	no
唐山大地震（1976年）	Tangshan Earthquake (1976)	no
1976年7月28日，中国河北省唐山市和丰南县在16小时内发生两次7级以上强烈地震。	On July 28, 1976, two powerful earthquakes of magnitude 7 or higher occurred within 16 hours in Tangshan City and Fengnan County, Hebei Province, China.	no
震源距地面23千米。	The epicenter was 23 kilometers above the ground.	no
唐山市全市交通、通讯、供水、供电中断，顷刻间被夷为平地。	Transportation, communication, water supply and power supply were interrupted in the city of Tangshan, which was razed to the ground in an instant.	no
140公里外的首都北京也有强烈震感。	Strong tremors were also felt 140 kilometers away in the capital, Beijing.	no
据官方统计，包括北京、天津在内的所有受灾地区，地震造成242769人死亡，164851人重伤。	According to official statistics, the earthquake killed 242,769 people and seriously injured 164,851 in all affected areas, including Beijing and Tianjin.	no
唐山大地震成为中国有记录至今第二多人死亡的地震，仅次于1556年嘉靖大地震。	The Tangshan earthquake became the second deadliest earthquake on record in China to date, after the 1556 Jiajing earthquake.	no
但是有海外科学家估计，这场地震可能造成至少65万人死亡。	But some overseas scientists estimate that the quake could have killed at least 650,000 people.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most destructive earthquake to hit the world in 60 years	no
印度洋大地震（2004年）	Indian Ocean earthquake (2004)	no
2004年12月26日，印尼苏门答腊岛亚齐省西岸160公里处发生地震，震源深度30公里，矩震级9.1到9.3。	On December 26, 2004, an earthquake struck 160 kilometers off the west coast of Aceh province on the island of Sumatra, Indonesia, at a depth of 30 kilometers, with a moment magnitude of 9.1 to 9.3.	no
地震引发了浪高高度达15到30米的巨大海啸。	The earthquake triggered a huge tsunami with wave heights of 15 to 30 meters.	no
太平洋沿岸总共14个国家被波及，其中受灾严重最严重的地区包括印尼亚齐省、泰国镐立和普吉岛渡假区、斯里兰卡和印度泰米尔邦。	A total of 14 countries along the Pacific coast were affected, with the worst hit areas including Aceh province in Indonesia, the resort areas of Ho Chi Minh and Phuket in Thailand, Sri Lanka and the Indian state of Tamil.	no
当时正值圣诞节的旅游旺季，受灾地区聚集了大量的旅客和本地居民，导致许多在沙滩上享受假期的旅客和在海边工作的当地人被海啸卷到海底，使这次地震不少人成为失踪者。	It was during the peak tourist season of Christmas, and the affected area was crowded with travelers and local residents, causing many travelers enjoying their vacation on the beach and locals working on the beach to be swept under the sea by the tsunami, making many people missing from this earthquake.	no
据估计，罹难人数和失踪人数至少有30万人。	The number of dead and missing is estimated to be at least 300,000 people.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most destructive earthquake to hit the world in 60 years	no
汶川大地震（2008年）	Wenchuan Earthquake (2008)	no
2008年5月12日，中国四川省汶川地区发生大地震。	On May 12, 2008, a massive earthquake struck the Wenchuan region of China's Sichuan Province.	no
根据中国地震局的数据，此次地震的面波震级达8.2级、矩震级达8.3级，破坏地区超过10万平方公里。	According to the China Earthquake Administration, the quake had a magnitude of 8.2 on the surface wave scale and 8.3 on the moment scale, damaging an area of more than 100,000 square kilometers.	no
截至2008年9月25日，地震共计造成69227人遇难，17923人失踪，374643人不同程度受伤，1993.03万人失去住所，受灾总人口达4625.6万人。	As of September 25, 2008, a total of 69,227 people had been killed, 17,923 were missing, 374,643 were injured to varying degrees, 199,300 people had lost their homes, and the total number of people affected by the earthquake was 46,256,000 people.	no
是中华人民共和国成立以来破坏力最大的地震，也是唐山大地震后伤亡最惨重的一次。	It was the most destructive earthquake since the founding of the People's Republic of China and the deadliest since the Tangshan earthquake.	no
2009年3月，中国国务院宣布将每年的5月12日定为防灾减灾日，加强对民众的教育和对防灾减灾工作的关注。	In March 2009, China's State Council announced that May 12 of each year would be designated as Disaster Prevention and Mitigation Day, to strengthen education for the public and focus on disaster prevention and mitigation efforts.	no
之后中国多地政府和中小学在每年这一天举行防震演习。	Since then, many governments and primary and secondary schools in China have held earthquake drills on this day every year.	no
中小学也开始重视普及“防震减灾”教育。	Primary and secondary schools have also begun to emphasize the popularization of "earthquake prevention and mitigation" education.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most destructive earthquake to hit the world in 60 years	no
海地地震（2010年）	Haiti earthquake (2010)	no
2010年1月12日，加勒比海岛国海地发生里氏7.0级的地震。	On January 12, 2010, an earthquake measuring 7.0 on the Richter scale struck the Caribbean island nation of Haiti.	no
震中位于海地首都太子港以西南方25公里，震源距离地表13千米左右。	The epicenter of the earthquake was located 25 kilometers south-southwest of Port-au-Prince, the capital of Haiti, and the epicenter was about 13 kilometers from the surface.	no
国际红十字会估计，受到地震影响的人口大约为300万。	The International Red Cross estimates that the population affected by the earthquake is approximately 3 million.	no
海地政府公布的确认死亡人数超过20万。	The Haitian government has announced a confirmed death toll of more than 200,000 people.	no
海地国内的一些地区，多达90%的房屋在地震中被摧毁。	In some areas within Haiti, as many as 90 percent of the homes were destroyed in the earthquake.	no
虽然国际社会提供了大量援助和支持，但是这个人口过剩腐败横行的贫困国家从未从这场灾难中恢复过来。	Despite massive assistance and support from the international community, the impoverished country, overpopulated and riddled with corruption, never recovered from the disaster.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most destructive earthquake to hit the world in 60 years	no
日本东北大地震（2011年）	Tohoku Earthquake in Japan (2011)	no
2011年3月11日日本东北地方外海发生矩震级为9.0的大型逆冲区地震。	On March 11, 2011, a large inversion zone earthquake with a moment magnitude of 9.0 occurred off the Tohoku region of Japan.	no
震中位于在宫城县首府仙台市以东的太平洋海域，震源深度测得数据为24千米，并且引发最大爬高40.1米的巨大海啸。	The epicenter of the earthquake was located in the Pacific Ocean east of Sendai, the capital of Miyagi Prefecture, and the depth of the quake was measured at 24 kilometers, triggering a huge tsunami with a maximum height of 40.1 meters.	no
这场地震是日本有观测纪录到以来第一个震级超过9的地震。	The quake was the first earthquake with a magnitude of more than 9 in Japan's recorded history.	no
约有2.2万人在灾害丧生，大约40万座建筑被完全摧毁或倒塌。	About 22,000 people lost their lives in the disaster and about 400,000 buildings were completely destroyed or collapsed.	no
福岛第一核电站受地震海啸影响发生泄漏事故。	The Fukushima Daiichi nuclear power plant suffered a leak due to the earthquake and tsunami.	no
这次事故在国际核事件分级表（INES）中被分类为最严重的7级。	The accident was categorized as the most serious level 7 on the International Nuclear Event Scale (INES).	no
福岛核事故导致在全世界都测量到微量辐射性物质，包括碘-131、铯-137（半衰期为30年）在内。	As a result of the Fukushima nuclear accident, trace amounts of radioactive substances, including iodine-131 and cesium-137 (with a half-life of 30 years), have been measured all over the world.	no
大量放射性同位素因此核事故释入太平洋。	A large number of radioisotopes were released into the Pacific Ocean as a result of the nuclear accident.	no
根据联合国的统计，在土叙两国灾区，目前至少有87万人急需食物。	According to the United Nations, at least 870,000 people are currently in urgent need of food in the affected areas of Turkey and Syria.	no
仅仅在叙利亚，就有多达530万人因为地震而失去家园。	In Syria alone, as many as 5.3 million people have lost their homes to earthquakes.	no
世界粮食计划署（WFP）呼吁拨款7700万美元，为土耳其和叙利亚因为地震而流离失所的灾民提供食物。	The World Food Program (WFP) has appealed for $77 million to feed victims displaced by the earthquake in Turkey and Syria.	no
目前灾区气温低至零下，很多灾民没有住所。	Temperatures in the affected areas are currently below zero, and many victims are without shelter.	no
土耳其政府分发了大量的热餐、帐篷和毯子，但是这些物资仍然难以送达很多急需帮助的人。	The Turkish government has distributed large quantities of hot meals, tents and blankets, but these supplies are still struggling to reach many people in desperate need.	no
而在深陷内战泥潭长达12年之久的叙利亚，地震则使民众的苦难处境雪上加霜。	In Syria, which has been mired in civil war for 12 years, the earthquake added to the suffering of the population.	no
在地震发生后的四天内，世界粮食计划署已经向土耳其和叙利亚的11.5万人提供了食物救济。	In the four days since the earthquake, the World Food Program has provided food relief to 115,000 people in Turkey and Syria.	no
世界卫生组织（WHO）则送去了72吨用于外伤处理和紧急手术的医药物资。	For its part, the World Health Organization (WHO) sent 72 tons of medical supplies for trauma care and emergency surgery.	no

NEWS GOV-MO: 警情通告：司警局呼吁市民提防假冒电讯公司诈骗短讯	NEWS GOV-MO: Police Notice: SZPD urges citizens to beware of fraudulent SMS from fake telecommunication companies	yes
近日司警局接获多宗电信诈骗案，不法分子假冒本澳电讯公司向事主发送附有网站连结的诈骗短信，以积分到期须尽快换领奖赏为饵，诱骗事主登入虚假网站进行兑换。	Recently, the SFPD has received a number of cases of telecommunication fraud in which criminals, posing as local telecommunication companies, send fraudulent SMS with links to websites to lure customers to log in to fraudulent websites for redemption under the bait that they must redeem their bonus points as soon as possible after their points expire.	yes
事主按指示输入信用卡资料及验证码，随即收到金融机构通知信用卡出现不明消费记录，怀疑信用卡资料经上述网站被盗取。	The victim entered his credit card information and verification code as instructed, and then received a notification from the financial institution that there were unidentified purchase records on his credit card and that he suspected that his credit card information had been stolen through the above website.	yes
经查，证实相关电讯公司并无发出上述短讯。	Upon checking, it was confirmed that the relevant telecommunications company had not sent the said SMS.	yes
司警局呼吁市民，如接获类似手机短讯须提高警惕，切勿登入短讯所载网站连结或提供任何个人资料；若被要求提供信用卡资料、帐户交易密码、交易验证码，更要加倍谨慎，防止信用卡被盗刷。	The SFPD urges members of the public to be vigilant if they receive similar SMS messages on their cell phones, and not to log in to the website link contained in the message or provide any personal information; if they are asked to provide credit card information, account transaction passwords, transaction verification codes, they should be doubly cautious in order to prevent credit card theft.	yes
防骗提示：	Fraud Prevention Tip:	yes
1. 多关注网络安全资讯，提高个人防范意识；	1. Pay more attention to information on network security and raise your awareness of personal precautions;	yes
2. 切勿随便登入来历不明的网站并在网站内登记个人及信用卡资料，以防遭人盗用；	2. Do not log on to websites of unknown origin and register your personal and credit card information on such websites to prevent unauthorized use;	yes
3. 警惕假冒网站及钓鱼网站，时刻留意网站网址是否与官方网站完全相符；	3. Be wary of fake and phishing websites, and always look out for website URLs that match the official website exactly;	yes
4. 为手机、移动装置或电脑安装防毒软件，并定期更新；	4. Install anti-virus software for your cell phone, mobile device or computer and update it regularly;	yes
5. 怀疑遇到诈骗或其他犯罪时，应立即致电司警局防诈骗查询热线8800 7777或报案热线993求助。	5. If you suspect that you have encountered fraud or other crimes, you should immediately call the fraud prevention inquiry hotline of the Police Department at 8800 7777 or the crime reporting hotline at 993 for assistance.	no
NEWS GOV-MO: 香港大型考察团走访澳门旅游景点设施 吸引港客并拓展港澳“联线同游”	NEWS GOV-MO: Hong Kong delegation visits Macau's tourist attractions and facilities Attracting Hong Kong tourists and expanding "joint tours" between Hong Kong and Macau	yes
旅游局组织由香港政府旅游部门、旅游业界及传媒代表组成超过100人的大型香港考察团到澳门，两天(10日及11日)的日程除了工作会议和业界洽谈，香港旅行社业界及传媒代表更分批走访澳门多个旅游景点、酒店及旅游相关设施，为香港市场引进最新的澳门旅游产品，同时促进两地文旅联动，共拓港澳“联线同游”市场。	MGTO organized a large-scale Hong Kong delegation comprising over 100 members from the tourism sector, travel trade and media representatives of the Hong Kong Government to Macau. In addition to working meetings and trade negotiations, the Hong Kong travel trade and media representatives visited a number of tourist attractions, hotels and tourism-related facilities in Macau in batches during the two-day (10th and 11th) programme, so as to introduce the latest Macau tourism products to the Hong Kong market and promote the cultural and tourism linkage between the two places at the same time. At the same time, it will also promote the cultural and tourism linkage between the two places, and jointly develop the market of "joint tours" between Hong Kong and Macau.	yes
亲临考察引入澳门旅游新玩法	Introducing new ways to play Macau's tourism with a personal visit	yes
是次香港百人大型考察团包括香港政府旅游相关部门领导主管、60多位来自旅行社及港澳跨境交通营运商的代表以及约30位分别来自旅游杂志及报章的记者、旅游社交媒体、网络媒体代表及博客/网红等，亲临澳门交流考察，了解澳门最新旅游资源，香港业界及媒体将澳门旅游的新玩法带给香港居民以至访港旅客，藉香港交通枢纽的优势，拓展港澳“联线同游”市场。	This large-scale delegation of 100 Hong Kong people, including the heads of tourism-related departments of the Hong Kong Government, more than 60 representatives from travel agencies and cross-border transportation operators in Hong Kong and Macao, as well as about 30 journalists from travel magazines and newspapers, representatives from travel social media, online media, and bloggers/web celebrities, etc., came to Macao for exchange and inspection, to learn about Macao's latest tourism resources, and for Hong Kong's travel trade and media to bring Macao tourism's new ways of play to Hong Kong residents and visitors. The Hong Kong trade and media brought new ways of Macau tourism to Hong Kong residents and tourists visiting Hong Kong, taking advantage of Hong Kong's transportation hub to expand the market of Hong Kong-Macau "joint tours".	yes

吸引香港旅客 拓展港澳“联线同游”	Attracting Hong Kong tourists and expanding "joint tours" between Hong Kong and Macao	yes

The two sides also discussed to jointly develop the "joint tour" market in Hong Kong and Macao, and jointly explore the Mainland and overseas markets, so as to promote the recovery of tourism in the two places.	yes
