习近平回信勉励援中非中国医疗队队员 以仁心仁术造福当地人民 以实际行动讲好中国故事	Xi Jinping writes back to encourage members of China's medical team in China-Africa to benefit local people with their kind hearts and skills, and to tell China's story with practical actions.	yes
2023-02-11 13:09:10 [来源:新华社] [责编:李絮枫] 字体:【大 中 小】	2023-02-11 13:09:10 [Source:Xinhua] [Editor:Li Shufeng] Font:[Large Medium Small]	yes
新华社北京2月10日电 中共中央总书记、国家主席、中央军委主席习近平2月9日给第19批援助中非共和国的中国医疗队队员回信，向他们以及广大援外医疗队员致以问候并提出殷切期望。	BEIJING, Feb. 10 (Xinhua) -- Xi Jinping, general secretary of the Central Committee of the Communist Party of China (CPC), president of the People's Republic of China (PRC) and chairman of the Central Military Commission (CMC), replied to a letter to the members of the 19th batch of China's medical team assisting the Central African Republic (CAR) on Feb. 9, sending greetings to them as well as the general number of foreign-aided medical team members and putting forward their earnest expectations.	yes
习近平在回信中说，你们在中非克服工作生活上的困难，用心服务当地民众，既是救死扶伤的白衣天使，也是传递情谊的友好使者。	In his reply, Xi said that you have overcome difficulties in your work and life in Central Africa and served the local people with all your heart, not only as ambassadors in white clothes who save lives and help the injured, but also as ambassadors of friendship who pass on friendship.	yes
今年是中国援外医疗队派遣60周年，谨向正在和曾经执行援外医疗任务的同志们致以诚挚的慰问。	As this year marks the 60th anniversary of the dispatch of China's medical aid teams to foreign countries, I would like to extend my sincere condolences to the comrades who are carrying out and have carried out medical aid missions abroad.	yes
习近平指出，中国人民热爱和平、珍视生命，援外医疗就是生动的体现。	Xi pointed out that the Chinese people love peace and value life, and foreign medical assistance is a vivid manifestation of this.	yes

新加坡旅游业复苏强劲 入境旅客比2021年增长19倍	Singapore's Tourism Industry Recovers Strongly Inbound Arrivals Increase 19-Fold from 2021	yes
（综合11日电）新加坡旅游局近日公布，预计2023年到访新加坡的国际旅客人次可达1200万至1400万，将带来约180亿至210亿新元的旅游收益；旅客人次和旅游收入将恢复到2019年新冠疫情前约67%至75%的水平；2024年旅游业实现全面复苏的可能性很大。	(Consolidated 11) The Singapore Tourism Board (STB) recently announced that it expects international tourist arrivals to Singapore to reach 12 million to 14 million in 2023, which will bring in about S$18 billion to S$21 billion in tourism receipts; tourist arrivals and tourism receipts will recover to about 67% to 75% of the pre-Singaporean Crown Epidemic level of 2019; and there is a high likelihood that tourism will achieve a full recovery in 2024.	yes
2022年新加坡旅游市场逐步重新启动和恢复。	Gradual re-launch and recovery of the Singapore tourism market in 2022.	yes
新加坡旅游局最新发布的统计数据显示，2022年入境旅客从2021年的33.06万人次增长19倍，达到630万人次，超越旅游局早前预估的400万至600万人次，游客已经恢复至疫情前33%的水平。	The latest statistics released by the Singapore Tourism Board (STB) show that visitor arrivals in 2022 have increased 19-fold to 6.3 million from 330,600 in 2021, surpassing the STB's earlier estimate of 4 to 6 million, with tourists having recovered to 33 percent of their pre-epidemic levels.	yes
2022年1月至9月，新加坡旅游收入共计89.6亿新元，预计2022年全年旅游收入可达138亿至143亿新元，比2021年的18.9亿新元增长6倍至7倍，已经恢复到2019年新冠疫情前约50%至52%的水平。	From January to September 2022, Singapore's tourism revenue totaled S$8.96 billion, and is expected to reach S$13.8 billion to S$14.3 billion for the full year of 2022, a six- to seven-fold increase from S$1.89 billion in 2021, and has already recovered to about 50% to 52% of its pre-Singaporean Crown outbreak levels in 2019.	yes

A：2月3日美国劳工部公布2023年1月非农就业数据，新增非农就业51.7万人，大幅高于市场预期的18.9万人；失业率降至3.4%，为近50年以来的最低位；时薪同比增速4.4%，环比增速0.3%，略有放缓。	A: On February 3, the U.S. Department of Labor released January 2023 nonfarm payrolls data, adding 517,000 nonfarm payrolls, sharply higher than the market expectation of 189,000; the unemployment rate fell to 3.4%, the lowest in nearly 50 years; hourly wages grew at a rate of 4.4% year-on-year, and at a slightly slower rate of 0.3% year-on-year.	yes

2月10日，证监会公告称，“基金E账户”APP在各手机应用商店上架并开展公开试运行。	On February 10, the SFC announced that the "Fund E Account" APP had been put on the shelves of various cell phone application stores and launched a public trial run.	yes
据介绍，“基金E账户”为个人投资者提供公募基金账户及份额信息的“一站式”查询服务，旨在解决广大中小投资者遗忘账户、查询繁琐等行业服务痛点。	According to the introduction, "Fund E Account" provides individual investors with "one-stop" inquiry service for public fund account and share information, aiming at solving the pain points of the industry such as forgotten account and cumbersome inquiry for the majority of small and medium-sized investors.	yes
据Wind数据显示，截至2022年底，国内共有公募基金管理人156家，管理基金规模约26万亿元；公募基金份额登记机构167家，公募基金销售机构411家。	According to Wind data, as of the end of 2022, there were 156 public fund managers in the country, managing a fund size of about 26 trillion yuan; 167 public fund share registrars and 411 public fund sales organizations.	yes
各份额登记机构账户体系相互独立，缺乏行业统一的查询渠道。	The account systems of the share registrars are independent of each other and lack an industry-standardized access channel.	yes
有行业人士表示，2021年末我国基金投资者超过7.2亿人，也就是说，全国有一半人都投资了基金产品。	An industry source said that there were more than 720 million fund investors in China at the end of 2021, which means that half of the country has invested in fund products.	yes
此前，投资者需要通过不同销售机构查询购买情况，而通过“基金E账户”可以查询所有销售渠道购买的情况，持有基金情况一目了然。	Previously, investors needed to check their purchases through different sales organizations, but through the "Fund E Account", they can check their purchases through all sales channels and see at a glance the status of their fund holdings.	yes
“基金E账户”APP是什么？	What is the "Fund E Account" App?	no
据相关文件介绍，“基金E账户”APP 是中国结算经中国证监会批准开发建设的公募基金行业门户手机应用，可为投资者提供全市场公募基金产品场外份额持有情况的一站式查询。	According to the relevant documents, "Fund E Account" APP is a public fund industry portal mobile application developed and constructed by China Clearing and approved by China Securities Regulatory Commission (CSRC), which can provide investors with one-stop query on OTC shareholding of public fund products in the whole market.	no
投资者可以通过“基金E账户”方便、快捷地掌握自己通过全市场各销售渠道购买的各基金管理人旗下公募基金产品场外份额的持有情况，全面提升查询效率。	Through the "Fund E Account", investors can conveniently and quickly grasp the status of their holdings of over-the-counter shares of public fund products under various fund managers purchased through various sales channels in the market, which comprehensively enhances the efficiency of inquiry.	no
具体来说，投资者可以通过“基金E账户”查询到的信息包括：在全市场各公募基金管理人处开立的基金账户信息、在公募基金销售机构处开立的交易账户信息以及持有的包括公开募集证券投资基金以及证券公司设立管理的投资者人数不受200人限制的集合资产管理计划等产品的场外份额持有情况。	Specifically, the information that investors can inquire through "Fund E Account" includes: information on fund accounts opened with public fund managers in the entire market, information on trading accounts opened with public fund sales organizations, and information on OTC share holdings of products including publicly offered securities investment funds and pooled asset management plans set up and managed by securities firms with no limit of 200 investors. OTC share holdings in products such as publicly offered securities investment funds and pooled asset management plans managed by securities companies with no limit on the number of investors.	no
上海证券基金评价研究中心业务负责人刘亦千向经济观察网记者表示，投资者可以通过“基金E账户”App一站式获知其所有的场外公募基金持有情况，帮助其找回“被遗忘的资产”，更重要的是为客户实现了综合基金投资情况的全账户信息归集，帮助客户更及时、准确、完整的掌握自身投资情况，从而更好地优化自身的基金组合配置，更好地规划自身的财务安排。	Liu Yichian, business leader of Shanghai Securities Fund Evaluation and Research Center, told Economic Observer that investors can know all their OTC public fund holdings in one-stop through the "Fund E Account" App, which helps them find the "forgotten assets". What's more, it realizes the whole account information collection of comprehensive fund investment for customers, which helps customers grasp their own investment situation in a more timely, accurate and complete manner, so as to better optimize their own fund portfolio allocation and better plan their own financial arrangements.	no

”	"	no
记者根据证监会官网公示的“基金E账户”下载及使用说明相关文件进行了账户注册并完成查询，整个过程耗时仅几分钟，主要分为四步：用户注册、实名认证、基金账户绑定、公募基金查询。	The reporter according to the official website of the Securities and Futures Commission publicized the "Fund E account" download and use instructions related documents for account registration and complete the query, the whole process takes only a few minutes, mainly divided into four steps: user registration, real-name authentication, fund account binding, public fund-raising funds query.	no

当时，由于东德各地的抗议者要求民主和自由，共产党领导人被迫下台。	At that time, communist leaders were forced to step down as protesters across East Germany demanded democracy and freedom.	yes

阿拉斯加上空被击落的 “物体”究竟是什么？	What exactly was the "object" shot down over Alaska?	yes
扑朔迷离，猜测纷纷	Confusion and speculation abound	yes
美国军方周五（2月10日）下午再次动用美国最先进的隐身喷气战机F-22击落了一个在美国阿拉斯加上空飞行的尚未确定身份的物体。	The U.S. military once again used the F-22, America's most advanced stealth jet fighter, to shoot down an as-yet-unidentified object flying over the U.S. state of Alaska on Friday (Feb. 10) afternoon.	yes
击落的地点距离阿拉斯加海岸十英里。	The location of the shoot down was ten miles off the coast of Alaska.	yes
这是美军在不到一周的时间里第二次击落空中飞行物体。	This is the second time in less than a week that the U.S. military has shot down an airborne object.	yes
上周六，来自中国的一个间谍气球在美国领空上漂移数日后在美国南卡罗莱纳州沿岸附近上空被击毁。	On Saturday, a spy balloon from China was destroyed over the U.S. coast near South Carolina after drifting through U.S. airspace for several days.	yes
五角大楼说，第二个被击落的物体于周四晚上首次进入美国领空，在阿拉斯加东北部上空移动时被美国军方跟踪，飞行高度为1.2万米（4万英尺），其大小与一辆小型汽车差不多，与先前被击落的那个中国间谍气球相比要小很多。	The Pentagon said the second downed object, which first entered U.S. airspace on Thursday night, was tracked by the U.S. military as it moved over northeastern Alaska, flying at an altitude of 12,000 meters (40,000 feet) and was about the size of a small car, much smaller than the Chinese spy balloon that was shot down earlier.	yes
五角大楼还认为，目前没有迹象显示，这个物体是可操纵的。	The Pentagon also believes that there is no indication that the object is manipulable.	yes
白宫国家安全委员会战略沟通协调员约翰·科比周五表示，虽然这个在高空飞行的物体的具体样子尚不清楚，但它“对民航飞机的安全构成了合理的威胁”。	John Kirby, coordinator of strategic communications for the White House's National Security Council, said Friday that while the exact appearance of the object flying at high altitude was unclear, it "poses a legitimate threat to the safety of civil aircraft."	yes
科比表示，这个物体与美国境内发现的那个间谍气球不同，它上面没有悬挂“有效载荷”。	Kirby said the object was different from the spy balloon found in the U.S. in that it did not have a "payload" hanging from it.	yes
科比说，“我们把它称为一个‘物体’是我们目前能够作出的最好的描述”。	"We call it an 'object' is the best description we can make at this point", Kirby said.	no
拜登总统在下令击落这个物体之前听取了五角大楼的建议，他作出这个决定的时候“非常谨慎”，科比补充说。	President Biden took advice from the Pentagon before ordering the object shot down, and he made that decision "very carefully," Kirby added.	no
美国官方对这个物体的描述大致可以归纳为：大小相当于一辆小汽车，没有操纵杆，没有悬挂装置，飞行高度为一万米左右。	The official U.S. description of the object can be roughly summarized as being the size of a small car, with no joystick, no suspension, and flying at an altitude of about 10,000 meters.	no
但这些信息还无法回答基本问题，比如这个物体究竟是什么东西，它属于哪个国家，它在执行什么任务。	But this information does not yet answer basic questions, such as what exactly this object is, which country it belongs to, and what mission it is on.	no
目前网上许多的分析和猜测认为，这可能又是一只中国气球。	Much of the current analysis and speculation online suggests that this could be another Chinese balloon.	no

也有人把阿拉斯加的这个“物体”与“不明飞行物”（UFO）联系在一起。	Others have linked the Alaska "object" to "unidentified flying objects" (UFOs).	no

“将外星飞船与气象气球混为一谈的讽刺意味很令人惊讶，但这不值得引发一场星际冲突，”梅杰说。	"The irony of conflating an alien spacecraft with a weather balloon is surprising, but it's not worth starting an interstellar conflict," Major said.	no

最后收集在一起，冠名《当我们谈论爱情时我们在谈论什么》。	Finally collected together under the title What We Talk About When We Talk About Love.	yes
我想，这个小说集，以及它的标题，像是一种行为艺术，作者想表达的是，爱情不止是舞台上的悲欢离合，都市传说中的海枯石烂，也不只是你侬我侬的如胶似漆，爱情不止是以上也不应该被以上代表，爱情也是平淡如水的生活，枯燥无味的日复一日，也有对生活的无措，现实的逃避，未来的茫然。	I think this collection of stories, and its title, is like a kind of performance art, the author wants to express that love is more than just the sadness and joy on the stage, the urban legend of the sea and the rocks, and not just you and me like glue, love is more than the above nor should it be represented by the above, love is also a life as plain as water, boring day by day, there is also the life of the unpreparedness, the reality of the escape, the future of the The future is uncertain.	yes

这正是我不推荐阅读的原因，从审美的角度上讲，本书的文笔和情节都索然无味，除非你的生活惊涛骇浪或者甜蜜得如生活在糖果城堡，否则你得阅读时的感觉就是见怪不怪和无聊。	This is exactly why I don't recommend reading it; aesthetically, the writing and plot of this book are tasteless, and unless your life is amazing or sweet as living in a candy castle, you'll have to read it with the feeling that you've seen it all and are bored.	yes
